Ministry of Finance Bans Whole Sheet Plain Cigarette Paper

[Nanjing] The Luyu Regional Consolidated Tax Bureau reported to the Ministry of Finance that unscrupulous merchants were transporting whole sheets of plain cigarette paper to the interior for the production of illegally manufactured cigarettes. Large quantities are imported through customs from time to time, but the customs authorities claim that the customs regulations do not prohibit such imports. If such activity is to be banned, the Ministry of Finance should order the Director-General of Customs to instruct all customs offices to implement a unified ban. Furthermore, the Shandong and Henan Postal Administration also sent a letter to the ministry, stating that plain paper has never been prohibited from transport and should not be detained. After the Consolidated Tax Department reported the situation to the Ministry of Finance for verification, the Ministry of Finance issued a special order to the consolidated tax bureaus of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hebei, Shanxi, Chahar, and Suiyuan on the 2nd, stating that the ministry is currently drafting amendments to the regulations on the purchase and transport of cigarette paper and will include whole sheet cigarette paper in the ban to crack down on it. In addition to informing the Ministry of Transportation to notify the Directorate General of Posts to cooperate and ordering all customs offices to carefully inspect and detain such paper, and ordering the Luyu Regional Consolidated Tax Bureau to strictly investigate and crack down on smuggling, they must all comply. (2nd, Special Dispatch)

Ministry of Justice Interprets Ambiguities in the Company Law

[Nanjing] The Ministry of Industry and Commerce requested an interpretation of ambiguities in Article 100, Paragraph 3 of the Company Law. The Ministry of Justice's interpretation is as follows: According to Articles 109 and 114 of the Company Law, the issuance of shares by a limited liability company should occur after the conclusion of the incorporation meeting and registration. Article 100 concerns the regulations for convening the incorporation meeting, and the phrase "issuance of unregistered shares" in Paragraph 3 refers to acknowledging that the share certificate states that such shares will be issued in the future. It should not be interpreted as granting the right to issue shares at the time of convening the incorporation meeting. Please refer to this for verification. (2nd, Special Dispatch)

The current traffic situation in the city, with two public bus companies and various vehicles powered by manpower, machinery, and animals, is sufficient to meet the demand. In recent years, the lives of rickshaw pullers have become increasingly difficult. However, because the previously divided zones were mostly based on the defense areas of the stationed military commanders, the size was uneven. In particular, the fifth and third zones had too many counties under their jurisdiction. Furthermore, due to traffic congestion, organization and command were lacking in flexibility. Siamese King Announces Abdication

Bangkok The Siamese Public Gazette Bureau received a telegram from London stating that the Siamese King formally announced his abdication today. (2nd, Reuters Dispatch)

[London] The King of Siam had the intention to abdicate because of a conflict with the National Assembly. The Siamese government sent a delegation to England to persuade him to stay. Negotiations have been going on for several months. Later, the King proposed several conditions, which had to be accepted by the National Assembly before he would agree to return to the throne. It is now known that the Siamese National Assembly has rejected the King's demands. This news was learned directly by the King from Bangkok, not conveyed by the Siamese government delegation stationed in England. After receiving the news, the King has decided to announce his abdication. It is said that the abdication edict will be issued soon and is very brief, with two reasons given. (1) The King believes that those suspected of opposing the government should not be secretly tried by a special committee and then exiled or executed, but should be handed over to the ordinary courts for legal judgment. This has been rejected by the National Assembly. (2) The Constitution stipulates that half of the members of the National Assembly should be appointed by the government, but the National Assembly opposes this. Due to the above two conflicts with the National Assembly, the King decided to abdicate to apologize to the people of the country. It is said that the King will remain in England until June this year, or may go to Switzerland. However, he will not reside in England for a long time. (1st, Havas Dispatch)

The Saar Problem Resolved: An Element of European Peace

Hoping for Increased Franco-German Friendship and the Removal of Thorns

Saarbrücken - German Führer Hitler received military honors at the city hall this afternoon. After the review was completed, the celebration of gratitude began. The square in front of the city hall was packed with people, making it almost impossible to breathe. Police had to block all roads leading into the square. This plebiscite is more important for European peace than initially thought. Next, Propaganda Minister Goebbels spoke, saying that Germany is no longer a republic governed by profiteers, but a nation of honor. Then, the new Saar Administrative Chief, Bürckel, spoke, dispelling the fears of Saar religious believers that the authorities might interfere in church affairs, saying that the National Socialist Party has fully relinquished its own rights to the church, but these rights must not hinder National Socialism. Finally, Hitler stood up, and a deafening cheer erupted, lasting for several minutes. Hitler's speech stated, in brief, that he was extremely pleased to be with the Saar people during the first hour of their restored freedom. This is a day of joy for all of Germany, and he believes it is also a day of joy for all of Europe, as this matter can eliminate the greatest dangers that have afflicted the two major nations (France and Germany). We sincerely hope that our great neighbor is also prepared to join us in seeking peace. The two major nations must now be able to work together to remove all thorns from the path to peace. Those in power should now know that one nation can never tear another nation to pieces. Kindness is more powerful than any document. Today we celebrate together; tomorrow we will jointly manage Greater Germany. You should be honored to be invited to cooperate with us. The speeches of all the speakers were broadcast nationwide by radio. It is estimated that there are hundreds of thousands of Germans in this area who are armed or have been trained by the government. (1st, Reuters Telegraph)

Saarbrücken - Führer Hitler delivered a speech to a large crowd today, celebrating the Saar's recovery of its native soil, hoping for the progress of European peace and understanding, and the increase of Franco-German friendship. Hitler recognized that the resolution of the Saar problem is a major factor in the peace of the European continent. Hitler said, "I believe that after the plebiscite, Franco-German relations will have a significant improvement. Our neighbor (referring to France) hopes for peace, and shares the same enthusiasm as we do. Today is not only a day of happiness for Germany, but also a time of joy for Europe." [Paris] The Chamber of Deputies discussed the issue of women's suffrage today. The effect of this vote is not yet certain, as the Chamber of Deputies' approval must still be ratified by the Senate, which has always opposed women's right to be elected and believes that the right to vote and the right to be elected should be discussed separately. Therefore, the Senate may propose another amendment and submit it to the joint committee of the two houses on universal suffrage for review, which is also possible. However, there is no doubt that women's right to vote in municipal elections will ultimately be passed. (1st, Havas Telegraph)

Greek Revolution a Flash in the Pan

A Section of the Army and Navy Suddenly Launches a Rebellion

Government Forces Obey Orders, and the Rebellion is Quickly Suppressed

Athens - Several army officers occupied the Salamis arsenal in an attempt to rebel, but they have been suppressed by the government. The rebels have already surrendered, and order in the capital and other provinces is good. Prime Minister Tsaldaris recently issued a statement saying that a small number of troublemakers attempted to undermine the people's freedom, but they have been crushed by government forces. According to information obtained by our reporter, the rebels had been preparing to revolt for a long time. The original plan was to have troops stationed in Athens and other places launch the rebellion at the same time. Last night, several rebel officers implemented the original plan and attacked and occupied the Salamis arsenal. Unexpectedly, the Athens garrison was not incited, and the situation did not escalate. Government troops and rebels exchanged fire until late at night. The rebels were unable to hold out and eventually surrendered. Military locations and government offices in the capital are all guarded by troops. At present, the rebel movement in the army has completely failed. In the navy, two destroyers have surrendered, and a submarine that had joined the rebels is also surrendering to the government. There were rumors of a rebellion in the province of Salonica, but this has been officially denied by officials. (2nd, Havas Telegraph)

Athens - A mutiny occurred at the Salamis Arsenal tonight, aiming to restore General Plastiras, who is currently in exile abroad. If the Greek government had not suppressed it with lightning speed, it would have caused a new revolution. Supporters of Plastiras, led by officers stationed at Salamis, apparently intended to seize the arsenal and use the weapons to supply those who oppose the government. Martial law was declared here this morning. At the same time, the government issued a statement saying that it was capable of controlling the overall situation. However, by this afternoon, rumors spread that the fleet had fallen into the hands of the rebels and that five warships were trying to escape by night. The government was aware of this and immediately issued a radio warning to them, saying that if they tried to escape, they would be regarded as pirates. According to a certain newspaper, Italian warships in nearby waters have telegraphed their government for instructions. This afternoon, a large number of reinforcements arrived from various provinces, all spirited and singing all the way as they marched through the streets of Athens. The reinforcements arrived just in time, as the authorities received a report that a large detachment of the Republican Guard was responding to the rebels just as they were stationed in a new camp. The authorities immediately dispatched a large army to attack the rebels. After a fierce battle, the rebels were exhausted and surrendered. Artillery was used during the battle. Afterwards, the government issued another notice to reassure the people, stating that a few madmen had rebelled against the legitimate government of the country, but thanks to the loyal and courageous service of the troops, the rebellious and patriotic rebellion had been quelled. The government is now in complete control of the overall situation. A Reuters reporter interviewed the Greek Army Chief, who said that the government had sent aircraft to bomb warships that were assisting the rebels. The cruiser Averoff was hit and damaged. Now, except for a small battle in Athens, the entire land is loyal to the government. The Army Chief also said that the government troops suffered few casualties, and about ten rebels were killed. It is the intention of the people here that the Averoff is now trying to communicate with the island of Crete. The Greek government is now investigating whether the ship has this intention, because this move has great political significance. It is said that the cruiser Hilli and three destroyers are also in line with the Averoff. The planes that bombed the rebel ships have all returned to the capital. All the planes showed signs of having been in battle. (2nd, Reuters Telegraph)

Air Suicide, Lovers Die Together

Basel, Switzerland - A primary school teacher from Rohlingen and a young girl flew around the city in an airplane. In the middle of their flight, they suddenly jumped out of the plane and fell to the ground, both dying tragically. The cause is unknown. It is reported that a few days ago, the two daughters of the American Consul General in Naples, Italy, committed suicide by jumping out of a plane flying from London to Paris in mid-air. Today's tragedy is similar to the previous incident. Could suicide by airplane become a popular trend? (1st, Havas Telegraph)

(3) To order smokers in various counties to undergo rehabilitation. Except in cases of special circumstances that have been verified as true, those who are granted a postponement should be allowed to postpone rehabilitation. Those who resist the order and fail to appear should be arrested and forced to undergo rehabilitation. Those who feign illness and abscond without being apprehended should be reported for public wanted. In addition, smokers who travel to other places before the rehabilitation period should undergo rehabilitation when they return to their hometown. Analysis of the Italian-Ethiopian Conflict

— (Italian Correspondence)

The Radical Advancement of Italy's Southern Policy

Mediterranean Disputes Extend to East Africa

Italy is considered one of the world's major powers, but it lacks iron ore, coal, oil, cotton, and wool. In short, it lacks all natural resources. Other countries, such as England and France, have relatively abundant iron and coal mines. Germany still has a large coal-producing area. Therefore, Italy has no choice but to seek natural resources overseas to compensate for its domestic deficiencies. However, the Mediterranean coast—the nourishing ground of the European powers—and Africa have been divided up by England and France. Italy only has a barren piece of land in Libya. After the European war, England was entrusted with governing an area of 989,000 square miles with a population of 9,330,000, and France was entrusted with governing an area of 253,000 square miles with a population of 6,470,000. Italy obtained very little. Later, England's diplomatic measures were very clever and expressed concessions to Italy. In 1924, it ceded the area near the Jubba River in Italian Somaliland in East Africa to Italy. In 1925, it also sacrificed a piece of Egyptian land and ceded the Yarabu area to it. Therefore, there are no major rifts between England and Italy. France has always been unwilling to make concessions easily, and local disharmony still occurs from time to time in North Africa, causing minor disputes. At the end of last year, after the relations between Germany and France became very dangerous, France feared that Italy would continue to advocate the abrogation of the Treaty of Versailles, which would indirectly help Germany. Therefore, it decided to unite with Italy's diplomatic policy, which led to the Rome Accord of January 7th this year.

One month before the establishment of the Rome Accord—on December 5, 1934—the armies of the two countries, Italian Somaliland and Abyssinia, bordering on each other, had an armed conflict. This conflict, on the surface, was not of great significance. Both sides only lost one hundred thirty-odd soldiers and a number of wounded. Especially in Africa, it is not considered a major event. However, Africa now has only one independent country, Abyssinia, and it is closely connected to the colonies of England and France. The occurrence of this conflict was due to the joint survey committee of the British and Abyssinian boundary demarcation entering the undecided area of dispute between Italy and Abyssinia, which triggered this incident.

According to the Italian government, the initial attack was on the surveying team and never crossed the Abyssinian border, and there was no reason to cross the border. However, the Abyssinian garrison was equipped with machine guns and artillery, and maliciously mocked the Italian army. One person also raised his hand as a signal to provoke the Italian army. The Italian army originally had no intention of starting a war, so after reinforcements arrived and the Abyssinian army was defeated, the Italian army did not pursue them. Therefore, Italy made the following demands on Abyssinia: first, the Abyssinian government must formally apologize; second, it must compensate for the losses.

The Abyssinian version is just the opposite. It said that the Italian army invaded 75 miles into Abyssinian territory. In the Walal area of Abyssinia, armored vehicles, artillery, and airplanes were lined up, and the Abyssinian army was attacked without reason. One hundred and fifty Abyssinian soldiers were killed in action. The offensive was not launched by the Abyssinian army, but by the Italian army. Moreover, the Italian army planes dropped two bombs on the Abyssinian army as a signal, followed by the opening of machine guns and tanks charging towards the Abyssinian army. At that time, the Abyssinian army only had the minimum amount of self-defense and did not open machine guns or artillery to counterattack. Afterwards, Abyssinia brought the matter to the League of Nations and requested the League of Nations to make a judgment. It is not yet clear how the League of Nations will deal with this matter.

Why does Italy want to expand its influence in Abyssinia? It is for its lack of resources and trade markets. Whether from a geographical, historical, or present international relations perspective, especially in Africa, there is room for development, and the only place with a considerable connection with Italy is Abyssinia.

Abyssinia is a mountainous country in Africa, with an area of about 350,000 square miles and a population of about 10 million. It is considered a sparsely populated area in Africa. Its railway, from Djibouti to Addis Ababa, totaling 487 miles, was built with French capital (after the Rome Accord was established, it will be jointly managed with Italy). This is an entirely undeveloped land and an excellent market for the export of Italian products. At the same time, Abyssinia's animal husbandry is quite developed, which can supply wool, and agriculture is gradually improving, which can supply cotton. Other items such as animal hides, coffee, wax, cream, and ivory are all the things that Italy currently needs most. Furthermore, the metal minerals that Italy lacks—iron, copper, placer gold, coal, etc.—even if there are no specific discoveries at the moment, it is very promising based on the local geological conditions. Moreover, in 1883, Italy signed a treaty of friendship with Abyssinia, and Abyssinia was a protectorate of Italy. In 1896, the Italian army suffered a defeat, and the protectorate was abolished. Now that Italy has become a modern country, it wants to take the opportunity to revive its past historical relations. However, the Abyssinian people are good at fighting, and it is feared that they will not readily submit. (January 31st, Rome)

Establishment of the Wuchang Headquarters

Chiang's Admonitory Speech to All Staff

Personnel Choices for Various Department Heads Announced

Hankou Correspondence: To facilitate Commander Chiang of the Military Commission's command over the suppression of remnant bandits in various provinces, a headquarters has been specially established in Wuchang, with Zhang Xueliang as the Director in charge of all matters. The original Headquarters for the Suppression of Bandits in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui will be abolished simultaneously, so that authority can be unified. After receiving the order, Zhang Xueliang is simultaneously concluding affairs at the headquarters and preparing the new headquarters. As of February 28, the headquarters concluded its affairs. On March 1, the new headquarters was officially established. At 8:00 AM that morning, Director Zhang Xueliang and other staff members of the headquarters arrived at the headquarters. At 9:00 AM, Commander Chiang crossed the river from Hankou by special steamer and landed at the Pinghumen Wharf in Wuchang, proceeding directly to the headquarters. The military band played music in welcome, which was very enthusiastic. Guests attending were limited to Pacification Commissioner He Chengjun, Provincial Chairman Zhang Qun, former Chairman Xia Douyin, and a few others. At 10:00 AM, the establishment ceremony of the headquarters was held in the grand hall, with Commander Chiang presiding. After the ceremony, he delivered an admonitory speech, saying, "Zhongzheng believes that in order to implement the Three Principles of the People advocated by Mr. Sun Yat-sen, to revitalize the nation and save the country, the initial methods and most urgent tasks are none other than educating the people and governing the army. The future work of the headquarters should, on the one hand, intensify the suppression of remnant bandits, ensuring that they are annihilated within a limited time to eliminate this huge disaster for the country and the nation; on the other hand, it should pay attention to reforming society, boosting morale, and establishing a foundation for national rejuvenation. With this goal in mind, what Zhongzheng sees as urgent and is willing to promote with all his strength is, on the negative side, the suppression of opium; and on the positive side, the promotion of the New Life Movement. Regarding opium suppression, the six-year plan previously set by the headquarters is indeed an effective method for completely eradicating it. In the past year, the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui have made progress in banning cultivation. The provinces of Jiangxi and Zhejiang have completely eradicated opium seedlings in their entire territories, with particularly notable results. And the investigation of opium users and registration of opium addicts in Jiangsu Province have also been effectively carried out. In the future, we should continue to implement the original plan thoroughly, aiming to extend the existing achievements to all provinces and further achieve the goal of completely banning the trafficking, manufacturing, and consumption of opium. Time flies, and one year has already passed of the six-year deadline. This cannot but be expected from all comrades, public and private parties, and enlightened people across the country, to work together to assist. Since the New Life Movement was initiated by the Nanchang Headquarters last year, it has relied on the concerted efforts of various regions to deeply instill the concepts of this movement into people's hearts. The creation of a new national life will truly begin with this. In the future, comrades at the headquarters, in handling affairs, in addition to realizing the three principles of militarization, productionalization, and arts-ification stipulated in the New Life Movement's outline, should also pay attention to the promotion of labor and service. Zhongzheng believes that life only has true meaning when it is based on labor and aimed at service. In particular, everyone must be able to labor based on the concept of serving the country and society, so as to sweep away the past bad habits of laxity and disorganization in our nation and establish a strong and united atmosphere to save our country from its current poverty and difficulties. Educating the people through labor has shown remarkable results in the past, and benefiting others at one's own expense should become the fashion. The great cause of national rejuvenation must be based on the promotion of the New Life Movement and the popularization of labor and service. This is what I especially hope all comrades will do by setting an example and leading the compatriots across the country to do their part and rise up together to assist in achieving it. As for developing highway transportation, organizing the masses, and popularizing education, these have been the basic policies of bandit suppression since the establishment of the Nanchang Headquarters. All the work that has been devoted to but not yet completed in the past should continue to be implemented, and its meaning should be further enriched. In the past, the purpose of developing transportation was to facilitate bandit suppression; in the future, it should be to develop culture. In the past, the goal was to improve national knowledge and promote the popularization of mass education; in the future, education should be linked to various facilities in addition to being popularized, in order to complete the mission of educating the people and saving the country. The revolutionary cause is vast and significant, but the way to start should focus on the essentials. I hereby reveal the essentials and admonish my comrades to strive together." After the speech, the meeting adjourned. Commander Chiang immediately issued a handwritten decree appointing the key personnel, including Headquarters Director Zhang Xueliang, Chief of Staff Qian Dajun, Secretary-General Yang Yongtai, Director of the First Department Yan Xunfu, Deputy Director Liu Shoupeng, and Staff Officer; Director of the Second Department Xiong Zhongtao, Deputy Director Min Xiangfan, and Chief Manager; Director of the Third Department Mi Chunlin, Deputy Director Ma Zhaoqi, and Chief of General Affairs; Director of the Fourth Department Wu Jiaxiang (Deputy Director not yet appointed), and Chief Secretary; Director of the Fifth Department Gan Naiguang, Deputy Director Zhou Congzheng, and Chief of Party Affairs; Director of the Sixth Department Chen Zhenxian, Deputy Director Wen Qun, and Chief of Rural Relief; Director of the Seventh Department concurrently held by Yang Yongtai, Deputy Director Huang Weicai, and Chief of Finance, Audit, and Opium Suppression. Departments One, Two, and Three are under the control of the Chief of Staff; Departments Four, Five, Six, and Seven are under the control of the Secretary-General. In addition, Director of the Transportation Department Lin Xiang, Director of the Army Reorganization Department Chen Cheng, Director of the Political Training Department He Zhonghan, and Director of the Military Law Department Chen Enpu were also announced. However, the personnel choices for the Directors of the Transportation and Medical Departments have not yet been determined, possibly belonging to Yu Feipeng and Liu Ruiheng. The Headquarters Director is a General, the Directors of Departments One through Seven are Major Generals, and the Directors of the Transportation and other departments are Lieutenant Generals. After Chiang appointed the key personnel, he also summoned them individually, admonishing them with great care. At 12:00 PM, he crossed the river and returned to Hankou. At 2:00 PM in the afternoon, the various departments of the headquarters began to work, issuing the following telegram: "To the various Yuan, Bu, Hui in Nanjing, Military Commission, Pacification Commissioners of various provinces, governments of various provinces, municipal governments, general commanders, corps commanders, division commanders, and independent brigade commanders: The Wuchang Headquarters was established in Wuchang on March 1 and has begun to work. This is a special telegram for your information. Military Commission Chairman's Headquarters, East 未印," (March 1)

Bandit Troubles in Western Shanxi and Northern Shaanxi

The Peiping Military Council Sends Personnel for Inspection

Taiyuan Correspondence: The spread of Communist bandits in northern Shaanxi has been going on for a long time. The original troops in the area, in addition to the entire division of 囗囗囗, also transferred the 囗囗囗 unit stationed in Luoyang to assist in the suppression, hoping to eliminate them as soon as possible to avoid future troubles. However, transportation in the area is obstructed, and the bandit gangs rely on natural dangers. Sometimes they gather into groups, and sometimes they disperse into smaller units. Therefore, although the two divisions of 囗囗囗 and the various troops sent by Shaanxi Province have been encircling and suppressing them for half a year, it is still difficult to eradicate their roots. Moreover, the bandits in northern Shaanxi have not yet been eliminated, and bandit traces have appeared in western Shanxi. The robbery in Kelan in northern Shanxi last winter was indeed secretly connected with the bandits in Shaanxi. After strict precautions by the Shanxi army, it was quickly quelled. Yan Xishan, the Pacification Commissioner of Taiyuan, attaches great importance to this. In addition to appointing Yang Yaofang, the commander of the 71st Division, as the Garrison Commander of western Shanxi, overseeing his troops to be responsible for the defense of the various counties along the river in western Shanxi, and strictly blocking and suppressing them, he also instructed the Pacification Office and the Provincial Government to be particularly careful in selecting and dispatching military and political personnel to those counties, and to pay close attention to the bandit situation at any time. In order to understand the actual situation of the bandit areas in northern Shaanxi and western Shanxi, He Yingqin, the acting chairman of the Peiping Military Council, recently specially sent Mao Xuzhai, Yang Zhen, and staff member Bi Chongzhi to Taiyuan to inspect the areas in western Shanxi and northern Shaanxi. Mao and others arrived in Taiyuan three or four days ago and have repeatedly consulted with Jia Jingde, the secretary-general of the Pacification Office, Zhu Shouguang, the chief of staff, Xu Yongchang, the chairman of the Provincial Government, Liu Shaoting, the representative of Jing Yuexiu stationed in Taiyuan, and the authorities of the Military Reorganization Committee, and decided to go to Fenyang on the morning of the 26th and then to the counties of Qingjian and Yulin in northern Shaanxi for inspection. According to Mao, the trip is expected to take about two months. If time permits, he also plans to give separate talks to the stationed troops, instructing them on the strategy of bandit suppression. (25th)

Re-discussion of the War Zone Issue at the Tianjin Meeting

Talks Between Takahashi and Yin Rugeng

Replacement of the Security Team Not Yet Scheduled

Tianjin Correspondence: Regarding the war zone issue, the Chinese and Japanese sides previously met in Tianjin and Peiping to discuss and decide on the new Eastward deployment of the newly formed security team and the reorganization of the Yutian team. However, the implementation procedures were delayed because the Japanese side considered it necessary to ask for instructions from the Kwantung Army. Therefore, on February 17, Yi Wo specially went to Changchun to report to General Nami, the commander of the Kwantung Army. He returned to Yu on the 23rd and immediately telegraphed Takahashi, the military attache of the Peiping Embassy, to convey the message to Yin Tong and Yin Rugeng. The Yins believed that the Tianjin Japanese Garrison Headquarters and the Japanese Consulate General were involved in resolving various issues and that it was necessary to negotiate with them on the proposals. Also, because Yi Wo had a message to meet with Meijin in Tianjin, the Yins arrived in Tianjin by train on the evening of the 24th. Before departing, they invited Takahashi to Tianjin to hold joint talks. Takahashi arrived in Tianjin by train on the evening of the 25th. Because Tao Shangming was unable to arrive in time, only the two Yins visited Takahashi at the Tokiwa Ryokan in the Japanese Concession on the morning of the 26th to consult on the matter first. At noon, Takahashi hosted a casual meal for the two Yins at the Ryokan. In the afternoon, Takahashi and Yin Rugeng went to the Japanese barracks in Haiguang Temple to visit Sakai, the chief of staff of the Japanese army, and senior staff members Oki, Dosakabe, and Kawaguchi to exchange views. They then went to the Japanese Consulate General to visit Vice Consul Tanaka. That evening, Yin Tong and Yin Rugeng hosted a banquet for Takahashi, Kawaguchi, Oki, Dosakabe, and Tanaka at the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau's reception office on Route 33 in the French Concession. During the banquet, they discussed the matter again. Originally, they intended to discuss it thoroughly after Yi Wo arrived, but it was postponed until the 27th. Tao Shangming arrived in Tianjin early in the morning, and Yi Wo also telegraphed that he was unable to come due to business. Therefore, the Yins and Takahashi seriously negotiated at the Tokiwa Ryokan and concluded in the afternoon. According to the new proposal by the Japanese side, the discipline of the newly formed war zone security team before entering for replacement is unknown. In order to avoid unrest in the war zone, it was proposed to first send a small part to be stationed in the Luan-Yu Administrative Region. After a considerable period of time, if the new security team proves to be reliable, the rest will be sent in gradually. The transfer of the Yutian Security Supplementary Team must be stationed near the Peiping-Liaoning Railway line and must be stationed in one place. The Japanese side explained that the discipline of the team is not good. If they are stationed in locations outside the railway, it will be difficult to prevent and suppress accidents. Therefore, the new defense area should be near the railway line. The Japanese side's proposal clearly deviates from the previously agreed principles, so no decision was made. Another meeting is planned for the 28th. As for setting up a Security Commander, the War Zone Cleanup Committee made the request based on the Japanese side's requirements in order to facilitate the management of the war zone security team, not to be directly under the provincial government, but to be under the jurisdiction of the Committee. A Security Committee will be established within the Committee, and Zhu Shiqin will be responsible as the responsible member. There will be no Security Commander. Today, Takahashi told visitors after the meeting that the negotiations on various issues in the war zone today have made considerable progress and will be implemented step by step soon. The return of Ma Lan Yu and the Eastern Tombs has been decided in the short term. Currently, the exact date of return has not been determined because minor issues have not been resolved. (27th)

International Commercial Telegram

Reuters Special Commercial Telegram, March 2

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Due to the sharp fall in the exchange rate of the pound against the French franc, the price has risen by one shilling and nine and a half pence today, reaching a new high price of one hundred forty-six shillings and ten and a half pence.

London Silver Bullion: The price of silver has reached its highest price since 1928 today. The spot price is twenty-seven pence, up nine three seven five. The futures price is twenty-seven pence zero six two five, up eight seven five. There is a widespread buying spree in the market, but there are very few suppliers, which has caused the price of silver to rise sharply. India and speculators sold when prices rose. Market conditions at the close were uncertain.

Exchange Rates

Anglo-American: The pound continued to be sold on the London foreign exchange market, causing prices to plummet. The opening price of the Anglo-American exchange rate was four dollars eight and one-sixth two five cents, which was lower than yesterday's closing price by one two five cents. It then felt pressure and fell two cents to four dollars seven and nine-six two five cents in just forty minutes. At eleven o'clock, it fell another six two five cents to four dollars seven and nine cents. At this point, the market began to stabilize. At noon, it rebounded three seven five cents to four dollars seven and nine-three seven five cents. At the close, it rose another half cent to four dollars seven and nine-eight seven five cents.

Anglo-French: The opening price was 72 francs 40, which was lower than yesterday by sixteen pounds. It continued to fall by forty-seven pounds within an hour. Afterwards, the pressure was greatly reduced, and the noon price was 71 francs 90, which was three pounds lower than at eleven o'clock. This price remained unchanged until the afternoon close.

American-British: In the New York foreign exchange market, the American-British exchange rate also fell two and three seven five cents to four dollars seven and nine-one two five cents due to the sharp fall in the pound in the London market.

American-French: The exchange rate opened half a cent higher to six dollars six and six cents.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton: The cotton market was loose, and after a slight price drop, the market stabilized. Although there were rumors that the U.S. dollar would continue to devalue due to the high gold price in London, the market did not change much because of this.

Chicago Wheat: The wheat market was stable because demand from manufacturers was strong and because the weather in the southwest has not yet improved.

Liverpool Cotton: The cotton market was stable today. The closing price for May futures was 6.88, up five pounds.

Liverpool Wheat: The wheat market rose eight seven five cents this morning. The closing price was four shillings and eleven and a half pence.

Rubber

London: The rubber market price was stable today. The closing price for July-September futures was six and a half pence, up ○ six two five.

New York: The rubber market price had a slight downward trend.

Securities

New York: Securities prices were generally stable in the securities market today, with no obvious trends. The Dow Jones 30 Industrial Average rose nine pounds to 103.36. Trading was not heavy. The New York securities market prices are listed on the left.

Record of an Inspection in the Northwest

— By Special Correspondent Geng Ya

An Overview of the Recent Turmoil in Xinjiang (4)

Ma Zhongying's second entry into Xinjiang took place between late April and early May of the 22nd year [of the Republic, i.e., 1933]. Ma's forces mobilized over 7,000 men in successive waves, creating an even more imposing presence than before. This occurred shortly after the April 12th Incident [i.e., Chiang Kai-shek's Shanghai massacre], when the new provincial government of Xinjiang was struggling to manage a multitude of affairs. Adding to the chaos, uprisings were erupting everywhere and Hami was undefended, allowing Ma to advance deep into Xinjiang and directly threaten Hami. In June, Ma successively captured Mulih River, Guchengzi (Qitai), and other locations, seized firearms from Fuyuan, and advanced westward. Sheng Shicai, the border defense commissioner of the new Xinjiang provincial government, personally led a large army eastward on May 26th to intercept them. However, he only reached Santai when he learned of the fall of Gu[chengzi], Fu[yuan], and other places. Furthermore, Ma's brother, Zhongjie, had already advanced on the provincial capital. Sheng then shifted from defense to offense, engaging Ma's main force in fierce combat at Ziniquan on June 7th. The fighting was intense, resulting in casualties on both sides (estimated at around 2,000). Meanwhile, the Tungan [Hui] commander He Janiyas and others, along with Mamuti and his troops, defected from Ma's side and attacked him in support of the new government. Ma was subsequently defeated in what became known as the Battle of Ziniquan. According to provincial sources, He Janiyas and Mamuti broke with Ma because, firstly, Ma Zhongying harbored wild ambitions to seize Xinjiang and sever ties with the Republic of China, while He Janiyas aimed to improve the political system and secure freedom and equality under Chinese law for all ethnic groups. Secondly, Ma Zhongying was a rootless ambitious outsider whose forces were merely a motley collection of bandits willing to gamble everything, harming people of all ethnicities. In contrast, He Janiyas was a respected local leader whose troops were all local residents, and who gradually disapproved of Ma's actions, leading to a change in strategy. Furthermore, they witnessed the establishment of the new government, which appointed Manchuk Zhabu as a division commander and Xilike Bandi Aylin, Han Dabiya, Ololo Zhabu Noyintai, and others as brigade commanders, demonstrating equal participation in military and political power for all ethnic groups. The provincial authorities also explained to He and others that the new government's overthrow of Jin [Shuren, the former governor] and the initial alliance between the Tungan people and Ma Zhongying in hopes of reforming Xinjiang's administration had been a shared aspiration. Now that Jin had been overthrown and their wish fulfilled, they should cooperate with the new government. Although He and others had initially declared a "ten-year war," they ultimately had no specific objective. Therefore, they reversed course and cooperated with the provincial army. (He had previously surrendered to the provincial army once before Jin's downfall, and there was another instance of wavering in southern Xinjiang after the Ziniquan cooperation). Sheng then appointed He Janiyas as commander of the South Xinjiang Defense Command and Mamuti as a division commander, ordering them to march to southern Xinjiang to suppress the Tungan uprisings in various counties.

In the Battle of Ziniquan, Ma's forces suffered heavy casualties and lost over 1,000 firearms. They scattered in disarray, leading their remaining troops to flee through mountain passes and take refuge in Shanshan and Turpan. After Sheng's army recaptured Fuyuan, Gucheng, and Mulih River, they intended to pursue the retreating forces. However, they suddenly received news that a so-called "second coup" (the April 12th Incident being the first) was about to erupt in the provincial capital, with the target being the overthrow of Sheng. As a result, Sheng abandoned the pursuit and rushed back to the province under cover of night. Using a meeting as a pretext, he invited the masterminds Tao Mingyue, Li Xiaotian, and Chen Zhong to the provincial government garden and executed them by firing squad. (This time, the commander of the Altai Garrison, Ba Pinggutai, was involved, and he was betrayed by his subordinate Beketef, who informed on him. Ba was also arrested, and Beketef has since been promoted to the position of Commander-in-Chief for Bandit Suppression in Southern Xinjiang.)

Earlier, in the spring of the 22nd year [1933], the Turpan Incident occurred, with Ma Zhongying instigating Ma Shiming to occupy Turpan and Shanshan. At that time, the Southern Mountain leaders Ma Quanlu and Ma Dexiang were at odds with each other. Ma Dexiang eliminated Ma Quanlu and surrendered to the new provincial government. Sheng Shicai appointed him as a division commander. Ma Shiming, resenting Ma Dexiang's surrender, eliminated Ma Dexiang as well. Consequently, the Tungan and Hui forces in the Southern Mountains all came under Ma Shiming's control. During Ma Zhongying's second entry into Xinjiang, he arrived in Turpan and Shanshan and dispatched his deputy division commander Ma Heiying to the Southern Mountains to assist Ma Shiming. In July, Ma Heiying led over 4,000 troops to invade the provincial capital from the Ulabaiyin south and Taiping Canal areas. After Sheng's army launched a two-pronged attack, Ma's forces were defeated and fled to the Toksun area in the south. Having suffered repeated defeats, Ma Zhongying sought a period of rest and reorganization. He requested to surrender to Sheng. Sheng, also having other concerns, made concessions and appointed Ma as the East Road Garrison Commander, designating Hami's Zhenxi as the garrison area. The new provincial government agreed to provide all salaries, supplies, and uniforms according to regulations. Ma dispatched representatives to the province to negotiate while remaining in Turpan, actively making preparations. In September, he secretly sent Ma Heiying to the Ashan area to incite the Hui people to create disturbances in Tacheng and invade Emin, Suilai, and Hutubi counties as the West Road force. He also ordered Brigade Commander Ma, nicknamed "Black Han," to lead several thousand infantry from Daban City to occupy Jijicao as the South Road force. Ma Zhongying himself led his core elite cavalry brigade from Daban City to Shiyaozi, secretly crossed the Tianshan Mountains, and launched a surprise attack on Fuyuan as the East Road force. At that time, Zhang Peiyuan, the Yili Reclamation Commissioner, although appointed as a provincial committee member, division commander, and border defense assistant by the new provincial government after the April 12th Incident at the recommendation of the new provincial government to the central government, his loyalty to the new provincial government was questionable. Therefore, Ma also contacted Zhang in an attempt to coordinate an attack from all directions and encircle Dihua [Ürümqi], vowing to take Dihua as a base for sweeping across Xinjiang.

As reports of the impending crisis poured in, the provincial government, sensing the dire situation, first dispatched a crack force (said to be the Ashan Garrison) to reinforce Tacheng overnight. When the reinforcements arrived, the siege of Tacheng was lifted. Ma's deputy division commander Ma Heiying, commanding Li Fuxing and others, then fled through the Emin, Suilai, and Hutubi areas to harass Dihua. They clashed with Sheng's army, engaging in fierce battles for several days and nights. Li Fuxing was killed in action in Hutubi, and Ma Heiying was later wounded and died in Queergou. The West Road force was thus defeated. The South Road force was intercepted by Sheng's main force, cutting off their connection. Subsequently, a major battle took place in Daban City, resulting in a slight victory. Sheng's army then returned to reinforce the provincial defenses. Upon hearing of the defeats of the southwest forces, Ma did not lose heart. He sent representatives to Dihua to continue peace talks, while secretly mobilizing elite troops to launch a surprise attack on Fuyuan according to the original plan. While Dihua was the foundation of the new province, and Gucheng was an important town to the east, Fuyuan, although a small city, was situated between Dihua and Gucheng, making it a crucial point on the eastern front in the Dihua area. Capturing Fuyuan would easily lead to the fall of Gucheng, making it easier to take the provincial capital. Contrary to expectations, despite Fuyuan having been occupied by Ma once before, the officials and residents this time put up an extremely fierce defense. Ma besieged the city for nine days and eight nights, but ultimately failed to break through. (The defensive methods were innovative, and women and children worked hard, making it worthy of description. I will elaborate later.) Ma's forces suffered heavy casualties, but they continued to persevere in a final struggle, which can be described as stubborn.

Zhang Peiyuan, the Yili Reclamation Commissioner, had long been dissatisfied with the new government's policies. Having recently made contact with Ma, he began to act in opposition to it. Sheng sent Chen Deli (now the head of the Xinjiang Provincial Finance Department and concurrently the head of the Foreign Affairs Department), Guanglu (a Xibe, now the consul-general in Tashkent), and Zhao Shipeng (now the administrative chief of Tacheng) to procure materials, but they were all intercepted by Zhang's forces. Zhang, under the title of Commander-in-Chief of the North Xinjiang, denounced Sheng Shicai. In early December, he dispatched Brigade Commanders Yang Zhenzhong and Liang Zhihong, separately, to Tacheng and Usu to then merge at Suilai and advance westwards, to link up with Ma Zhongying's forces and threaten Dihua. Sheng's army also dispatched a portion of its forces westward, encountering Yang's forces in Wula Usu, part of the Suilai region. The two sides were locked in stalemate, with no clear victor. Yang and others suddenly received an urgent telegram from Zhang, ordering them to immediately return. Upon reaching Anjihai (six stations from Yili), Zhang had already committed suicide. After dispatching Yang and others, Zhang had only left a thousand men to guard Yili. At that time, the Altai and Tacheng Garrison units of Sheng's army, specially trained from among the local people, about two combined brigades of elite troops and equipment, under the command of a certain administrative chief of Tacheng, took advantage of Zhang's weakened rear defenses and launched a direct assault on Yili. They fiercely attacked Zhang's forces for three days and nights. Zhang, seeing that his position was untenable, committed suicide about sixty li outside the city. After his death, a will was found by the pursuing troops (the text of which roughly stated, "One mistake was trusting Minister Luo's visit to Yili, who claimed that he would provide substantial support. Another mistake was Yang Zhenzhong launching his attack too early and retreating too late. The enemy's artillery has been bombarding Yili for too long, and I feel deeply guilty. The merchants previously lent funds for military supplies, which should be repaid with my estate. My elderly mother is still alive, please dress her in mourning clothes when I am coffined," etc. However, there are also claims that Zhang's death was actually a murder, and that the will was forged.) After their victory in Yili, the Garrison troops boarded vehicles and advanced eastward. In the five counties they passed through—Usu, Shawan, Suilai, Hutubi, and Changji—the Garrison troops, unfamiliar with the local conditions and anxious to provide reinforcements due to the tight provincial defenses, failed to attend to everything, causing considerable disturbances along the way. At that time, Ma Zhongying, the Commander-in-Chief of South Xinjiang, who was corresponding with Zhang Peiyuan from afar, had mobilized over 10,000 troops and was besieging Dihua for a month.

During Ma's last siege of Dihua, he relied on the disturbances caused by Ma Heiying in the north, the response from Zhang Peiyuan in the south, and the successive additions of mutinous troops from Sheng's army (mostly former loyalists of Jin Shuren), making his power formidable. However, the vast expanse of Xinjiang and the inconvenient transportation greatly impacted military operations. Ma had already contacted the provincial government to surrender after his initial defeat, but Zhang's joint telegram denouncing Sheng arrived belatedly. Ma was also unaware of Ma Heiying's failure. Zhang Peiyuan's suicide was even further unknown to him. Therefore, he independently launched a large-scale siege of Dihua, which lasted for a month. The city faced shortages of food, and the crisis worsened daily. However, Sheng's army remained confident, shrinking the defensive perimeter to just over 20 li, adopting a strategy of "waiting for the enemy to tire," defending without attacking. On the dawn of December 17th, Ma's forces managed to breach the defense line from Nanliang in the south, but were quickly repelled. Later, hearing that the Altai Garrison reinforcements, loyal to Sheng, were approaching to launch a pincer attack, Ma gathered a large force to intercept them at Toutun River, 70 li west of the city, engaging the Garrison troops in a desperate battle. Ma led the remaining 4,000 to 5,000 troops in a chaotic retreat, fleeing towards southern Xinjiang.

After relieving the siege of Dihua, a portion of the Altai Garrison troops happily returned north by vehicles, while another portion, along with Commander Song's Rescue Army, pursued Ma's forces. Fierce battles erupted along the way. When encountering large cities or dangerous terrain, Ma would often defend and resist stubbornly. At Hala Gorge, between Yanqi and Turpan, the gorge was 30 li long and naturally treacherous. The pursuing troops used airplanes to drop bombs to break through. Meanwhile, He Janiyas's forces, ordered to intercept Ma's troops in the Kucha area, had their weapons seized by Ma's forces, reviving Ma's military strength. Later, after suffering successive blows, they retreated past Aksu and reached Shache. Out of desperation, Ma transferred the remaining command of his troops entirely to Yang Zhenzhong and Li Hairu, and lightly equipped, fled to the Soviet Union via Kashgar. Sheng repeatedly requested extradition, but the Soviet Union refused. After Ma's departure, Yang Zhenzhong, Li Hairu, and others led the remaining forces into Yutian. Yang and Li were former subordinates of Jin Shuren and had been under Sheng's command. Li surrendered to Ma when Gucheng fell, and Yang retreated south with Ma after Zhang Peiyuan's defeat. Ma gained significant assistance from Yang and Li. Before leaving, he had allegedly entrusted them to act as the acting commander and deputy commander of the 36th Division. At the end of the 23rd year [1934], the Dunhuang County government in Gansu still received a telegram from Yang and others denouncing Sheng, indicating that the new provincial government's orders had not yet reached the counties south of the Tarim Basin. (To be continued)

The Twists and Turns of the Hai River Rehabilitation Project

Slackness in the Engineering Rehabilitation Office

The National Economic Commission Should Speedily Reform

Tianjin Dispatch: The Hai River management has always been the most important water conservancy project in North China, and it is particularly important for the transportation and commerce of Tianjin Port. Over the years, the river management authorities have spared no expense, claiming to actively manage the river. Unfortunately, there have been unscrupulous elements among the leaders, coupled with various administrative obstacles, which have led to the deterioration of the river channel. If this continues, not only will past efforts be wasted, but the reduction in the river's discharge capacity will expose the million residents of Tianjin to the risk of flooding. The Dagu Shoal waterway is merely an extension of the Hai River, and it is also deteriorating daily, which will inevitably have a significant impact on China's North China economy. The North China Water Conservancy Commission previously formulated five measures for the Hai River remediation project. Subsequently, in the autumn of the 17th year [1928], the Construction Commission, the Ministry of Finance, the Hebei Provincial Government, and the Tianjin Municipal Government jointly organized the Hai River Rehabilitation Committee, and obtained approval from the National Government to issue 4 million yuan in Hai River Dredging Public Bonds, deciding to levy an additional tax on Tianjin Customs duties to serve as funds for repaying the public bonds. In the spring of the 18th year [1929], the Tianjin Customs surcharge began to be levied. The consular corps stationed in Tianjin took the opportunity to inquire about the affairs of the Rehabilitation Committee because foreigners were subject to tax obligations. Among the main engineering personnel of the committee, some took advantage of foreign influence to receive huge monthly salaries. As a result, salaries alone accounted for a staggering 1.6 million yuan. The remediation plan set by the committee originally involved purchasing low-lying areas in the Tahe River depression for the Yongding River floodwater to deposit silt, and then directing part of the clear water into the sea via the Jinzhong River, and another part into the Hai River via the newly opened river. This plan was originally very simple, and it was estimated at the time that it would take at most 18 months to complete. Who would have thought that it would be delayed again and again, and it was not until May of the 21st year [1932] that half of the sea entry project was completed. Seeing that millions of dollars had been spent, but the Hai River was still as silted as ever, at the end of the 21st year, there was a proposal to abolish the Rehabilitation Committee. Later, the government, at the request of Yu Xuezhong, extended it for another year to see the results. However, in addition to recommending to the government that the levy period for the customs surcharge should be extended and another 2 million yuan should be borrowed to complete the original remediation plan, the committee made no progress on the rehabilitation project. Therefore, in December of the 22nd year [1933], the government resolutely abolished the committee, and its uncompleted projects were taken over by the Engineering Rehabilitation Office, organized by the Ministry of Interior in conjunction with the Hebei Provincial Government. According to the outline of the rehabilitation measures determined at that time, all uncompleted projects were to be completed by the flood season of the 23rd year [1934], and extensions could be granted as appropriate if obstacles occurred in fact, but at most they could not exceed the end of December. As for the shortage of 1.92 million yuan in funding, the Ministry of Interior and the Hebei Provincial Government would jointly submit it to the Executive Yuan for approval to extend the Tianjin Customs Surcharge for allocation. In February of the 23rd year, the head of the Engineering Rehabilitation Office, Mao Yisheng, took office. Unexpectedly, Mao went into mourning for his father the day he took office, and was forced to leave Tianjin to attend the funeral. A certain person who held an important position in the Engineering Office of the Rehabilitation Committee and received a huge monthly salary, then resumed his old tricks, using foreign influence to achieve his manipulation and control. The most shocking thing is that on January 12th of this year [1934], the water dam at the mouth of the Yongding River Diversion Canal suddenly burst. Afterwards, someone personally went to the site of the newly breached river mouth for on-the-ground inspection, and it was said that this breach was quite different from a self-breach. Because if a water dam is eroded and breached by river water, the breach on the Yong River side must be inwardly curved into an arc. The two ends of the remaining dam at the river mouth are very straight, and the period of the river mouth opening was during the severe winter, when the earthen dam and river water had long been frozen, making it difficult to erode even if there was a large amount of water, let alone during a low-water period. According to residents of Ge Yu Cheng Town, near the river, someone took five or six crowbars from Zhenxing Hall on the evening of January 11th, pried open the dam, and because the water was not flowing smoothly, they took the crowbars again and widened the dam, resulting in the breach. Observing the current situation, after the newly opened diversion canal trough of the Yongding River is filled and closed in the future, a slight rise in water will inevitably lead to overflow on both the north and south sides, making it difficult to restore the current river channel situation. Who instigated this matter has not yet been ascertained. Fortunately, the government, in view of the need to unify the various water conservancy agencies, has agreed on the outline of the measures for unifying water conservancy administration and undertakings. All original water conservancy agencies in each watershed will be uniformly taken over by the National Economic Commission for overall planning, allocation, and management. The Engineering Rehabilitation Office is a temporary organization, and should be terminated as soon as the project is completed. The Economic Commission bears the heavy responsibility of unifying the national water conservancy agencies, and should promptly carry out thorough reform and find improvement methods, so that the Hai River remediation project, which the people of North China are eagerly awaiting, can be completed as soon as possible, and Tianjin, known as China's second largest port, can flourish. (February 25)

Changes in the Administrative System of Fujian Province

Tightened Budgets for Various Counties

Streamlined Agencies Eliminated

Fuzhou Dispatch: The Fujian Provincial Government has recently made several changes to its administrative system, which are described below: (1) Revision of County Grading and Funding: The counties in the province are divided into three grades, with the first-grade counties divided into two levels: Grade A includes 14 counties: Minhou, Putian, Jinjiang, Longxi, Changle, Fu'an, Nanping, Xianyou, Tong'an, Zhangpu, Longyan, Changting, Shaowu, and Pucheng, with a monthly budget of 2,500 yuan; Grade B includes 4 counties: Fuqing, Xiapu, Zhao'an, and Nan'an, with a monthly budget of 2,200 yuan. Second-grade counties include 21 counties: Hui'an, Yongchun, Lianjiang, Gutian, Fuding, Ningde, Haicheng, Zhangping, Anxi, Shunchang, Shaxian, Youxi, Yong'an, Jianyang, Songxi, Zhenghe, Jianning, Liancheng, Shangyuan, Yongding, and Wuping, with a monthly budget of 1,940 yuan. Third-grade counties are also divided into two levels: Grade A includes 16 counties: Luoyuan, Minqing, Yongtai, Nanjing, Changtai, Pinghe, Yunxiao, Dongshan, Jiangle, Ninghua, Datian, Dehua, Siming, Chong'an, and Jinmen, with a monthly budget of 1,570 yuan; Grade B includes 7 counties: Pingnan, Shouning, Qingliu, Mingxi, Taining, Hua'an, and Ningyang, with a monthly budget of 1,380 yuan. (2) Remote areas of various counties, such as Dahu in Minhou, Yingqian in Changle, Nanri in Fuqing, Zhou Dun and Sandu in Ningde, Anhai in Jinjiang, Maxiang in Tong'an, Shima in Longxi, and Yangkou in Shunchang, previously had county assistants or public security bureaus to assist the county government in managing affairs. Due to financial difficulties, they were abolished. Now, it is planned to imitate the organizational methods of the Jiangxi Special District Political Bureau, taking into account local conditions, and first establish political bureaus in six places: Nanri, Sandu, Zhou Dun, Anhai, Maxiang, and Yangkou. Under the command of the administrative commissioner in charge, the bureaus will handle police, financial, construction, and security affairs within their jurisdiction. The internal organization of the bureaus will consist of one director, four assistants, and two or three employees, with a monthly budget of 650 yuan. (3) In terms of financial administration, it has been decided to streamline redundant agencies to concentrate authority and save expenses. Local taxes, except for large and special ones, will be handled by the county governments. A total of 109 bureaus and offices will be eliminated, retaining only nine tax bureaus: Minhou, Siming, Jinjiang, Longxi, Putian, Jian'ou, Fuchang, Hangyong, and Zhuqi. This will save more than 419,000 yuan per year. As for the Seventh District (Longyan) and Eighth District (Changting) Financial Reorganization Offices in the recovered areas of western Fujian, the administrative commissioners of the districts, Chen Yifeng and Lin Sixian, serve concurrently as directors, and the Department of Finance sends Lin Zhaohong and Qi Jue as accounting directors. According to reports, the offices have been organized and will be established on March 1. (February 27)

Xiamen Real Estate Plunges

Land Prices Fall to 40-50% But Still No Buyers

Nearly One-Third of Shops Are Vacant

Xiamen Dispatch: Since the Navy established the Road Administration in the Xiamen urban area in the 16th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1927], it has actively developed roads, built embankments and parks, and opened up residential markets, which caused land prices to soar. The 19th year [1930] was the golden age of real estate. At that time, all those engaged in real estate made huge profits. By the 21st year [1932], the communists occupied Zhangzhou, and property owners became wary. Those who had not invested in real estate held back, and those who had already invested sold off their properties. In the past one or two years, Nanyang [Southeast Asian] trade has declined sharply, and remittances from overseas Chinese have decreased significantly. Moreover, overseas Chinese capital is also nearing depletion. Xiamen real estate was originally mostly invested by overseas Chinese, so land prices have fallen drastically. From last winter to this spring, Xiamen's commerce has been depressed, finance has been difficult, and rents have plummeted, yet many properties remain vacant. As a result, real estate and houses have become increasingly neglected. Recalling the 19th and 20th years [1930-1931], land prices on Datong Road and Zhongshan Road were sold for more than 3,000 or 5,000 yuan per square zhang [a traditional unit of area]. Now, they have fallen to 30-40% of that price, and mortgages are at 25%, yet there are still no buyers at any price. The grounding of the Xiamen Bank and the collapse of large money shops such as Yufeng and Jianyuan this spring were the result of investing in real estate or engaging in real estate mortgages. According to a recent official survey, in the market center of Zhongshan Road, 37 shops are vacant. On Datong Road, 68 shops are vacant. The only section with relatively few vacancies is the section of Siming South Road from Siming Theater to the intersection of Zhongshan Road. On the rest of the coast, 33 shops are vacant on Lujiang Road. On Tongwen, Chenguang, and Hutoushan Roads, 68 shops are vacant. On Siming East and North Roads, there are more than 20 vacancies each. On average, the number of vacant shops on each road accounts for about one-third of the total. In the brothel area of Siming South Road, Dashi, 50 shops are vacant, accounting for half of the total. It is remembered that a row of more than ten Renji shop buildings on Datong Road was offered for 400,000 yuan by Chen Guohui before the 21st year [1932], but the deal fell through because the middleman demanded 20,000 yuan. Recently, it was offered for sale at 180,000 yuan, but still no buyer. From this, one can know the state of commerce in Xiamen. (February 28)

Kunshan

District Chief Wanted, Property Confiscated

Wang Wuqing, the district chief of the Eighth District, has extensive social connections and spends lavishly. During his five years in office, he has embezzled a considerable amount of district funds. The amount of funds embezzled for the single item of disaster relief has already reached more than 7,000 yuan. After being discovered by the provincial committee, Peng Baichuan, the county magistrate of Kunshan County, dispatched police to summon the district chief to the county for questioning, but Wang had already escaped. The county government then submitted a report to the province to issue a warrant for his arrest and to recover the embezzled funds. It is now learned that the county government has discovered that Wang has real estate in the name of Wang Hanchen (the district chief's father), consisting of over 800 mu of farmland and a residence covering four mu, valued at approximately 40,000 to 50,000 yuan, which has been confiscated in preparation for auctioning it off to repay the debt. However, Wang had long separated from his brother, and all the farmland in his own name had already been mortgaged. Now that the county government has confiscated everything, it is said that all the creditors are in a panic.

Songjiang

Shelter Prevents Enticement and Lewd Schemes

Last year, Wangdian, Xiashi, and other places in Jiaxing Prefecture, Zhejiang Province, were affected by drought, resulting in a poor harvest. Farmers, young and old, accompanied by their families, traveled to Songjiang in groups to seek food. This county first had the relief agency send personnel to provide daily rations. Then, Zhou Xuewen and Zhu Jiuwang, directors of the Mountain Red Cross Branch, acting out of neighborly benevolence, opened a shelter at Chao Guo Temple, providing the refugees from Zhejiang Province with food and lodging. Some of them went out to seek relief. Among the refugees were young women who, although pale, were relatively beautiful, and some people took the opportunity to seduce them. The staff of the shelter found that Wang Chen, a refugee aged 28, was escorted back to the shelter every evening by Zhou Gengsheng, a local man, in a suspicious manner, fearing there might be an enticement going on. The man and the woman were sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. As a result, there were no grounds to accuse them of enticement, but to prevent any possible harm, it was decided to hand Wang Chen over to her aunt, Wang Jiang, to take her back to her home, and the association would pay her fare home. Zhou Gengsheng, who has been running a small stall at the station, was detained for three days as a warning because of his improper behavior.

Suzhou

Various Industries Jointly Petition for Reduction of Property Tax

The Wu County South Goods Industry, Timber Industry, Chinese and Foreign Cloth Industry, Silk Industry, and more than ten other industry guilds, recognizing that Wu County's property tax is divided into two types: one for businesses at ten percent of the property value, and one for residents at five percent of the property value, both with an additional 15% levy for security expenses. After the Security Corps was reorganized into the Provincial Security Brigade last year, local figures had already petitioned and received approval from the provincial authorities to cease the additional levy for security expenses starting from the 24th year. Unexpectedly, it was recently reported that the Finance Department issued an order stipulating that property tax for businesses must be 15% of the property value and 8% for residents, an increase over the previous rate. In the midst of the current economic downturn, people simply cannot afford the burden. Furthermore, there are more than twenty counties in Jiangsu that have not yet implemented property tax. Why then increase the tax rate for counties that have already implemented it? This seems unfair. Therefore, they have jointly sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce to forward to the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments, requesting a reduction in the tax to ease the burden.

Reactionary Elements Cause Trouble in Suzhou

Suzhou's various theaters have recently received threatening letters from a self-proclaimed "White Blood Group Communist General Group." The details of this have already been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the Da Guangming Cinema in the North District of the city also received a letter from the group yesterday, threatening to extort 5,000 yuan, with a two-day deadline for payment and a prohibition on reporting to the authorities. After receiving the letter, the cinema immediately secretly reported it to the Second Sub-bureau. Huang Tianyi, the chief of the sub-bureau, has dispatched plainclothes police to investigate secretly. Zhang, the chief of the Public Security Bureau, believes that reactionary elements are attempting to cause trouble in Suzhou, but because the matter concerns local tranquility, he has secretly ordered the detective team to pay close attention, it is said.

Industry Representatives Petition Regarding Business Tax

The Wu County Business Tax Bureau has recently dispatched a large number of officials to various stores to urge them to fill out declaration forms and will directly audit accounts on a household-by-household basis. The County Chamber of Commerce is deeply concerned about this matter, fearing that misunderstandings may arise. Therefore, on the afternoon of the first day, they convened a meeting of industry representatives. The chairman was Cheng Ganqing. All representatives agreed that the business and capital amounts for the 23rd year had already been declared for the county's business tax, and the 24th year had not yet begun. At this time, there was no need to urge the filling out of declaration forms or audit accounts. Eight people, including Pan Ziqi, Shen Bingzhang, Zhang Shoupeng, Fan Junbo, Xu Xiaozhai, and Ji Xiaosong, were immediately elected as representatives. Yesterday (the second day) at noon, they first went to the County Party Headquarters and the County Government to petition. The County Magistrate of Wu County received them. The Special Commissioner Sun and the Chief of the Public Security Bureau Zhang were both at the County Government at the time and met with them simultaneously. The representatives explained their intentions and requested a delay in the investigation. The County Magistrate of Wu County agreed to consult with Guo, the Chief of the Business Tax Bureau, to handle the matter. The representatives then left.

Changshu

Drama Troupe Member Entices Two Female Students

Since last winter, Tan Huang opera has become popular here, with four new troupes appearing within a month. The performers all come from elsewhere. Recently, two female students were abducted at the same time. One was Weng Shuzhen, the niece of Weng Zhenbo, the current section chief of the Nanjing Military Commission, a graduate of the County Girls' High School. Because she went to watch the opera every day, she was enticed into an adulterous relationship by Jiang Yueming, a member of the Xin Guang Opera Troupe. Later, through Weng, she introduced Xi Ruiyu, a third-year student at the County Girls' High School, and they formed an inseparable bond. The two girls, passionately in love, stole everything they had and quietly left Changshu together, hiding in the Central Hotel in Changzhou. Recently, the families of both have been searching everywhere and have reported to the detective team for assistance, but without any trace. Now, the man and women, having run out of money, Xi accompanied Jiang back to Changshu to find a solution, while Weng remained in Changzhou. When they returned to Changshu, they were arrested by the detective team and transferred to the County Government by the Public Security Bureau for questioning on the first day. According to Xi, she is seventeen years old and was easily tempted by Jiang because of her youth and weak will. When questioned, Jiang Yueming denied enticing her. He was immediately ordered to be detained. As for Weng Shuzhen in Changzhou, the authorities used a long-distance telephone to instruct the county to keep her there and wait for her family to come and claim her.

Crackdown on Opium Den, Assaulting Police and Resisting Arrest

The County Public Security Bureau received a secret report yesterday that Sun Caizhi had privately established an opium den inside the No. 11 doorplate of Huishan Zhijie Street for people to smoke opium, and requested the arrest. At about 3:00 p.m., the temporary inspector Feng Yimao, led four police officers from the car patrol team, went to search the address. Sun Caizhi, and three smoking customers, including Sun Ronggen, were arrested on the spot, along with opium pipes and lamps. Just as they were about to take them to the bureau, Liu Sanda led more than ten hooligans who came to the scene and beat the police officers and snatched the three opium offenders. Feng Yimao, seeing the situation was not good, immediately arrested Liu Sanda, the leader of the robbers, and sent a police telegram to the headquarters for assistance. The Inspector General Wang immediately dispatched the police chief Zhu Bangzhao, leading more than ten police officers from the car patrol team, to the rescue. When the gang saw a large number of police officers coming, they fled in all directions. Subsequently, Feng Yimao chased and caught Song Jintang and Pan Tingmei, who assaulted the police and robbed the prisoners, at Xishan, and took them to the bureau for interrogation. Petition to Prohibit Speculative Trading in Exchanges

The Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation held a meeting in Wuxi on the 21st of last month. The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce proposed to prevent speculative trading of cotton yarn and to protect industry. The proposal was passed according to the original plan. Yesterday, the Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation telegraphed the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Industry and the Shanghai Cotton Industry Control Committee, stating: "The Shanghai Chinese Cotton and Cloth Exchange's daily transactions are all short sales, and speculators gather there, causing the market value of domestically produced cotton yarn and cloth to fluctuate day and night, shaking in this whirlpool of panic and unable to stabilize. The most serious thing is that the market value of cotton yarn is reversed, and the exchange buys and sells short, focusing on speculation, the market loses its balance, and the situation is on the verge of collapse. Shanghai factories cannot maintain themselves and are closing down one after another. Inland yarn factories, especially in Wuxi, cannot be ignored. This matter concerns the lifeline of the national yarn factory and the livelihood of workers, which is extremely important and significant. It is proposed to forward to the central government to strictly prohibit speculative trading of cotton yarn in exchanges, in order to balance the market and protect the yarn industry. The executive and supervisory meeting of the Association discussed and agreed that the establishment of the exchange was originally intended to regulate supply and demand and equalize prices. In all countries around the world with cotton production, the exchange has never priced cotton yarn and cotton at the same time, fearing that speculation and manipulation would harm the root. For example, Japan auctions yarn but not cotton, and the United Kingdom and the United States auction cotton but not yarn, which are clear examples. However, the Shanghai Chinese Cotton and Cloth Exchange auctions both cotton yarn and cotton at the same time, allowing speculators to succeed in their monopolistic manipulation. The price of cotton is auctioned higher and higher. According to the current calculation of the spot yarn price of the standard cotton, each bale of cotton yarn has to lose more than 20 yuan. The yarn industry is related to the national foundation, and it is necessary to maintain it. The yarn and cloth exchange is named and registered with yarn and cloth products, and it should be the principle of auctioning yarn and cloth. It should not abandon cloth and infringe on the raw material of cotton for yarn and cloth. This distinction is very clear. The country maintains the industry, and it is important to reverse the decline. It is proposed to order the Shanghai Chinese Cotton and Cloth Exchange to maintain a balance between the auction prices of cotton yarn. If the manufacturing costs of the 20-count standard yarn, calculated by the market weight of 430 kilograms of standard cotton (excluding unified tax, less than 45 yuan), should immediately stop the auction or directly stop the cotton trading to stabilize the cotton market and protect the industry.
