Yu Feipeng Received the Press Yesterday

Published Written Remarks on His Impressions of the Inspection

Praised the Progress of Transportation Equipment in Europe and America

According to the Central News Agency, Yu Feipeng and his party of five from the transportation group of the Military Transportation Inspection Team returned to the country and arrived in Shanghai on the first day. Yu and others will stay in Shanghai for ten days. Yu also received reporters from various newspapers at his private residence on Baylor Road at 3:00 p.m. yesterday and issued a

Written Statement

saying, "I was ordered to go abroad in May of last year to inspect various transportation policies, and traveled with General Xu Tingyao of the Ministry of Military Affairs. After arriving in Europe, I visited England, the United States, France, Italy, Germany, Soviet Russia, Poland, Austria, and Czechoslovakia. I crossed the United States from England in January of this year and returned to China yesterday. My companions were Commander Jiang Ou, Chief Engineer Wei Yifu, Engineer Wu Baofeng, and Engineer Chen Xu. General Xu and his party started from Europe and will arrive in Shanghai before the 10th of this month. During this tour of Europe and the United States, all the countries we visited gave us various conveniences, so the progress was smooth. The transportation industries in Europe and the United States, such as road, telegraph, postal, and shipping construction, are very complete. Whether in large cities or remote locations, there are almost always various transportation facilities. Now that science is developed and technology is advanced, various countries are also conducting intensive research and vigorous progress in new transportation construction. Regarding railways, (1) is the improvement of steam locomotives, which increases speed and saves fuel. (2) is the internal combustion engine train, which is formally undergoing testing. Its speed can reach 110 miles per hour. In addition, regarding expenses, (1) is the standardization of machinery. Since the procedures are fixed, replenishment is naturally convenient. (2) is the mechanized train assembly yard, which works quickly. (3) is the railway repair shop. (4) is the old material utilization factory, which is considered to save costs in every possible way. Furthermore, various countries are making every effort to build highways. No matter how remote a place is, there is a highway to reach it. Now there are about 9 million miles of highways and about 33.4 million cars in the world, which is a truly amazing record. Regarding the telegraphic administration, (1) is wireless radio facsimile. Since the invention of this kind of facsimile, it only takes six or seven minutes to send and receive from Europe to the United States. (2) is ultra-high frequency radio, which is also being tested. (3) is carrier wave telegraph and telephone. This kind of equipment can simultaneously send 18 telegrams on a pair of lines. (4) is television, which is also being actively tested and can be used for broadcasting television. (5) is a telephone that uses telegraph. This kind of machine is very useful. In addition, various countries are developing long-distance telephones more universally and rapidly. Regarding the postal service, the tidiness and speed of the internal equipment of its organs need not be discussed. Even if we look at the promotion of rural postal services, there is almost no place that cannot be reached by mail, and the convenience can be imagined. In addition, for long-distance mail, there is airmail, and even ordinary letters can be delivered by air. The prosperous cities also have air transport pipe equipment for mail, and the speed is indescribable. Regarding shipping administration, although the tonnage of ships was large before the European War, the utility was limited. After the European War, the tonnage decreased, and the utility increased, because the ships were rebuilt, the equipment was perfect, and the speed was increased. This is one. After the European War, the inland rivers were greatly dredged, and navigation was extremely convenient, and the number of ships over 100 tons was greatly increased. This is two. From the above, it can be seen that European and American countries use science to carry out various new transportation constructions, and their advantages are worthy of reference. My impression after the inspection is excellent, and I also think that the reason why European and American countries attach great importance to transportation is that transportation has a major and close relationship with politics, military affairs, and economics, and is the foundation of the country's lifeline. Now, taking advantage of the opportunity to talk to you, I will briefly describe the general situation. The detailed situation will be submitted to the government in a formal report."

Joint Banquet

Yu is scheduled to stay in Shanghai for ten days before going to Beijing to visit President Wang of the Executive Yuan and Minister Zhu of the Ministry of Communications, and then to Hubei to visit Chairman Jiang to report the details of the trip. The local Merchants Bureau, Eurasia China Airlines, International Telecommunications Bureau, and Shanghai Telegraph Bureau and other agencies hosted a public banquet at Liu Hongsheng's residence on Julida Road at 6:00 p.m. last night to welcome Yu. The guests and hosts enjoyed themselves. Mayor Wu and others are also scheduled to host a banquet for Yu in the next few days, it is said.

Inspection Schedule

In terms of telecommunications, the International Telecommunication Bureau and the Radio Station one day, the Telegraph Bureau and the Electrical Material Storage and Transfer Office one day, the Telegraph Bureau and the Ministry's Material Storage Committee one day. In terms of postal services, the Postal Remittance and Storage Bureau one day, the Postal Administration General Supply Office and the Postal Administration Bureau together one day. In terms of shipping, the China Merchants Bureau General Office one day, the No. 4 Wharf Repair Factory one day, the Shipping Administration Bureau in the morning, and the Wusong Merchant Ship School in the afternoon together one day. In terms of aviation, China Aviation Corporation and Eurasia Aviation Corporation together one day. Qian Chengxu Goes to Shandong at the Summons of Han

Conveniently Lectures for About Ten Days Before Returning to Shanghai

Qian Chengxu, Secretary-General of the China Industrial Federation, went to the United States last year at the invitation of the United States to lecture and inspect the country's light industry. He returned to Shanghai in October. Han Fuju, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, and Shen Honglie, Mayor of Qingdao, telegraphed Qian to invite him to Shandong for negotiations. Later, it could not be done due to matters. Now Chairman Han has again urged him by telegram. Qian is leaving for Lu today at 8:00 a.m. on the early express train. A reporter from New Voice News inquired about the purpose of the trip. According to him, Shandong Province is the only supply area for industrial raw materials in China, so it has a chronic trade deficit. In the first half of last year, because there were many transactions between places, various payments were generally able to be received after the due date, and there was no feeling of difficult circumstances. However, since June, problems have occurred with silver, the market has tightened currency, transactions have been scarce, freight has been stagnant, and the economy has been affected. The current economic organization has two systems: (1) financial capital, (2) industrial capital. The financial capital of all countries in the world is direct, and the industrial organization is horizontal, echoing each other and increasing the chips. Although China's financial capital organization has a history of nine years, the industrial capital organization is still in its infancy. To increase market chips, industrial capital must work hard to increase chips before it can overcome this extraordinary difficulty. Furthermore, China is a manufacturing country with a huge domestic market, and its economic situation is not comparable to that of England and Japan. It must promote the sales of goods abroad. Therefore, in this situation, it is not necessary to adopt a progressive currency expansion step. There are other forces to maintain its self-sufficiency and self-supply status. Shandong has the possibility of developing industrial capital, and the implementation steps must first organize material storage warehouses, use the remaining raw materials of farmers, and provide a certain amount as the warehouse reserve. If a considerable amount is obtained, material price securities can be issued. Shanxi has actively advocated the organization of warehouses. Last year, it was discussed with Chairman Han, because there was no urgent need in fact. Now that there is a shortage of chips on the market, the establishment of warehouses can no longer be delayed. Therefore, I will go to Jinan and Qingdao to talk with Chairman Han and Mayor Shen. Moreover, the markets in Qingdao and Jinan need to cooperate with Shanghai. After the method is determined in the future, the leaders of the financial and industrial sectors of the city will be invited to Lu to negotiate, it is said. It is also heard that after Qian arrives in Lu, he plans to give lectures on economics for two days, and will stay for about ten days before returning to Shanghai, it is said.

Hunan Province Implements Ban on Rice Export

Promulgated from March 1st

Hunan rice has always been sold to Guangdong and Ningbo. Currently, there are still a lot of people from these two groups who has already purchased rice, and it has not yet been shipped. Recently, the price of rice in Hunan has soared suddenly, and the selling price per stone has exceeded 11 yuan (but the rice stone is larger than in Shanghai). The people of Hunan are panicking. The provincial authorities have proposed to abolish the export permits for rice in order to relieve the rice shortage and protect the food supply of the province. The provincial government has ordered that the policy of blocking food exports from the province will be implemented from March 1st. Hunan rice will not be allowed to be shipped out of Hunan from the date of promulgation of the ban, and can only be circulated and supplied within the province. Yesterday, this port has received a telegram from Changsha, saying that the export ban on food has been promulgated, and those who have already purchased it but have not yet shipped it are afraid that they will not be able to ship it.

江南 Railway Company Undertakes Jing City Railway

Contract Signed, Lease Term Twenty Years, Monthly Rent Three Thousand

Personnel Dispatched to Beijing to Take Over, Transfer to be Completed Within a Week

The Jiangnan Railway Joint-Stock Company on Foch Road in this city considers Nanjing as China's capital, and transportation is quite important. Therefore, after consultation with the Beijing Municipal Government, it has leased the Beijing City Railway to enrich and develop it. The lease contract has been formally signed, and on the first day, personnel were dispatched to Beijing to take over. A reporter from the New News Agency recorded the contract as follows:

Contract Signed

The Jiangnan Railway Company and the Beijing Municipal Government, after several consultations, have agreed on the lease contract for the Beijing City Railway, totaling ten articles. The contract has been formally signed at the Beijing Municipal Government. The signing representatives were Shi Ying, the Mayor of Beijing, and Zhang Jingjiang, the General Manager of the Jiangnan Railway Company. The witnesses included Wu Zhihui, a member of the Central Committee, Lai Lian, the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, Xiong Tingling, the Secretary, Zhang Jianming, a Councilor, as well as managers and technicians from the Jiangnan Railway Company, all of whom participated in the listing. It has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for record. The Jiangnan Company also dispatched personnel to take over on the first day, and the takeover is expected to be fully completed within a week.

Lease Term Twenty Years

The main content of the contract is as follows: (1) The Nanjing Municipal Government agrees, from the date of establishment of this contract, to lease all properties and equipment such as land, tracks, houses, and vehicles specified in the attachment of the Beijing City Railway to the Jiangnan Railway Company for use. However, the width of the track land shall be 31.5 English feet as the standard. Where this number is insufficient, the original area shall be leased. The roadside shall be marked with a map separately. The station land shall be leased in its entirety according to the original land. (2) The Jiangnan Railway Company agrees, from the date of handover to the date of cancellation of the contract, to pay the Municipal Government a monthly rent of three thousand silver dollars per month. However, the deposit shall be repaid without interest upon the expiration of the contract. (3) Both parties agree that the lease period shall be twenty years, calculated from the date of handover. During the lease period, the Jiangnan Railway Company shall use it in good faith and maintain it properly.

Road Construction Project

(4) All properties and equipment such as land, tracks, houses, and vehicles shall be handed over clearly by the Municipal Government on the spot at the time of the establishment of this contract (the number and condition shall be attached to a separate list). On the date of expiration, the Railway Company shall return it to the Municipal Government according to the list. Except for natural consumption that cannot be preserved, if there are any shortages, compensation shall be paid according to the market price. At the expiration of the contract, the company shall not dismantle or request compensation from the Municipal Government for all ordinary equipment that has been replaced, such as tracks and sleepers. In addition, for equipment added by the company, if the Municipal Government agrees in advance, the Municipal Government may compensate the price. The rest shall be dismantled by the company itself upon expiration. (5) The road construction project from Zhongzheng Street to outside the South Gate shall be handled by the Jiangnan Railway Company. The Municipal Government shall do its best to assist. The Jiangnan Railway Company may request the Municipal Government to handle all procedures for requisitioning land along the Zhongzheng Street to South Gate route.

Submitted for Record

(6) During the effective period of this contract, neither party may terminate the contract halfway without the consent of the other party. If one party fails to fulfill this provision, the other party may demand compensation for considerable losses. One year before the expiration, if both parties agree, either party may notify the other party to cancel the contract upon expiration, but they may also negotiate renewal methods. (7) If the Jiangnan Railway Company is willing to purchase all the assets of the Municipal Railway, it may, at any time, consult with the Municipal Government and agree that both parties will jointly assess the price, establish a transaction, and sign a contract, and the lease contract will be canceled immediately. (8) This contract shall be prepared in triplicate, with each party holding one copy as proof, and the other copy shall be submitted by the Municipal Government to the Executive Yuan for record. (9) This contract shall take effect immediately after being signed by both parties and recorded by the Executive Yuan. (10) The handover date is tentatively set for March 1.

Negotiations for More Than a Year Have Ended

Afterwards, the Blue Funnel Line issued a loss bill, totaling more than 131,000 yuan for repairs and other items, and repeatedly demanded compensation from the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The First Half of the Ji'an Steamer Has Been Shipped to Shanghai

This Kind of Salvage Work

Is Still Pioneering in Shanghai

The Zi Lin Report stated that the Ji'an steamer, which sailed from Hankou and ran aground and broke on Tongzhou Island on January 11 (220 feet long, 40 feet wide, 1788 tons, built by Yesson Shipyard in 1907), has had its first half transported to Shanghai this morning (2nd) after seven weeks of work by Chinese and foreign experts and divers, with the assistance of the tugboats Socie and Agrout. The Socie, carrying this "special cargo", arrived at Songkou after dusk yesterday, and is expected to sail into the Huangpu River this morning. This is a pioneering move in Shanghai. With such achievements in mechanical and salvage work, it is worthy of being the fifth largest port in the world. It was originally planned to tie the two sections of the Ji'an ship to the left and right sides of the Socie and transport them to Shanghai at the same time, but because the second half was in a special position, the cargo in the cabin could not be cleared for a while. It was decided to transport the first half to Shanghai first, and the second half will also be transported within a few weeks. This time, the Far Eastern Salvage Company worked for six weeks to remove the cargo from the first half and transport it to Shanghai for sale. Then the water in the cabin was pumped out with a water pump, and the first half was able to float. During the transfer of the rear cargo, the floating first half was used as a storage place. A few days ago, the keel of the ship was shortened with a chemical flame. Since the water quality of the Yangtze River is turbid and contains sand, it is extremely difficult for divers to work underwater. Now experts are still trying to isolate the exposed part of the rear section from the water, and drill a hole in the deck, from which the goods are taken out and transported to Shanghai at any time.

The Social Bureau's Investigation Confirms That There Are More Than 700,000 Workers in Shanghai

Divided into Three Categories: Industry, Commerce, and Transportation

The Investigation Has Been Completed and the Report Has Begun to Be Prepared

The New Voice News Agency stated that the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, in view of the fact that there has never been a statistic on workers in Shanghai, specially commissioned the Benefiting Workers Division of the Third Section to organize a general survey of workers in Shanghai. Since it began in June last year, the survey has been completed and the report has begun to be prepared. It is divided into three categories: (1) industrial workers, (2) commercial workers, and (3) transportation workers. The bureau has investigated industrial workers many times in the past, but it is not very complete. Commercial and transportation workers have never been investigated. This time it took several months to complete the investigation. There are a total of about 700,000 workers in the city.

The Central News Agency stated that after the British HSBC Bank arbitrarily auctioned off the Shenxin No. 7 Factory, the Chinese people unanimously fought for it. The government also telegraphed the local authorities in this city by the Executive Yuan to assist in the handling. In the past few days, the future of the negotiations has gradually revealed a glimmer of hope. A reporter from the Central News Agency has compiled the news obtained yesterday as follows:

Kong Will Return to Shanghai

According to a telegram from Hankou, Mr. and Mrs. Song and Kong flew to Hankou to visit Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to discuss financial issues, which have come to an end and will return to Shanghai by the original plane within days. It is reported that Kong will come to Shanghai after meeting with President Wang in Beijing to discuss the issue of rescuing the Shenxin No. 7 Factory.

HSBC Expressed

The attitude of HSBC is due to the unanimous support of all sectors of our country, fearing that it will affect Sino-British relations. It has clearly stated that if Shenxin has a solution, the auction contract that has been established can also be withdrawn. It is rumored that the two Japanese lawyers Okamoto and Nakamura represent non-Japanese merchants.

Prepare to Redeem

The Central News Agency's Nanjing telegram on the 2nd stated that regarding the redemption of the Shenxin No. 7 Yarn Factory, the Ministry of Finance and Industry has actively planned rescue measures, and the Shanghai Municipal Government has worked hard to negotiate with HSBC Bank. The situation is very good. Roughly, the arrears of interest owed to the bank of 250,000 yuan will be allocated in advance, and the arrears will be fully repaid in four months in order to redeem the Shenxin Factory.

The Japanese Side Denies

The purchaser of this auction of Shenxin No. 7 Factory requested Japanese lawyers Okamoto and Murakami as representatives, so the general public regarded it as purchased by Japanese merchants. The Japanese Consul, in order to avoid causing resentment among the Chinese people who are improving Sino-Japanese relations, issued a statement the day before yesterday saying, "Regarding the auction of the Shenxin Textile Factory, some people have publicized that the buyer is a Japanese merchant. However, the results of the investigation by this consulate of Japanese yarn factories and companies have made it clear that the buyer is not Japanese. This is hereby declared."

Shenxin Situation

A reporter from the Central News Agency met with Rong Hongyuan, the son of Rong Zongjing of Shenxin Textile Company, yesterday. According to him, this issue can only be decided after Minister Kong of Finance comes to Shanghai. He also said that the company's yarn sales have been smooth recently, or it may be due to the Shenxin No. 7 Factory incident.

The Xinfeng Steamer Was Hit in Tianjin

But It Can Still Sail

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Northern Ocean Steamer Xinfeng, Fully Loaded with Passengers and Cargo, Has Been Unloaded After Arriving in Tianjin. After All The Goods Were Loaded in Tianjin, It Sailed Back to Shanghai. When The Ship Left Tianjin, The Japanese Rinnei Maru Steamer of The Japanese Seisei Marine Transportation Company, Which Operates Dalian and North China, Arrived in Tianjin. When The Xinfeng Was Started, It Was Hit By The Japanese Steamer. It Was Too Late to Avoid It at The Scene, Resulting in The Destruction of The Right Side of The Bow of The Xinfeng Ship. The Xinfeng Steamer Immediately Stopped Sailing. The Shipowner Jointly with The Tianjin Customs Harbor Master and The Shipowner of The Japanese Ship, Went to The Xinfeng Ship to Survey The Loss. It Was Estimated That There Was a Hole in The Iron Plate of The Outer Right Side of The Fore Cabin, and The Guardrail Wood and Railings on The Deck Were Also Damaged. On The One Hand, The Shanghai Office Reported, and on The Other Hand, The Negotiation Was Conducted with The Japanese Ship. However, The Damaged Part Was Above The Water Line, Which Did Not Affect Navigation. According to The Bureau's News, The Ship Can Still Sail Back to Shanghai and Has Sent a Letter to The Insurance Company for Verification.

Dalian Bay Wharf Area Restrictions on Navigation

(1) Setting Up Buoys (A) Buoy Position, From The Chimney (224 Feet) Southwest of Hamacho Pier, 59.75 Degrees Due North, Distance 5.02 Chains (Each 10 Chains Equals One Nautical Mile) Type, Red Wood Prismatic Buoy (B) Light Buoy Position, From The Chimney (224 Feet) Southwest of Hamacho Pier, 48 Degrees Due North, Distance 7.2 Chains, Abbreviated as Constant Red, Type Red Wood Prismatic Buoy, With a Constant Red Light Bulb (C) Light Buoy Position, Chimney (234 Feet) Southwest of Mobincho Pier, 56.25 Degrees Due North, Distance 7.8 Chains, Abbreviated as Constant Red, Type Red Conical Buoy, With a Constant Red Light Bulb (Note) In Addition to The Above Three Buoys, Which Mark The Filling Project of The Fourth Wharf, All Other Buoys Within The Scope Have Been Revoked. Nisshin Kisen Stevedores Demand a General Wage Increase of Six Yuan

The Company Agrees to a Discretionary Increase

Workers Decide to Negotiate Again

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the stevedores of Nisshin Kisen Company's various ships, dissatisfied with their current treatment by the company, requested the Seamen's Union to negotiate with the company for a wage increase of six yuan per person per month to maintain their livelihood. The union dispatched investigator Lu Rongzhi to contact the company multiple times, but without success. Therefore, the workers requested former Chinese manager Wang Yiting of the company to act as mediator. After Wang negotiated with the company repeatedly, the management agreed to consider the situation and make a discretionary increase, but could not fully accept the workers' demand for a general increase of six yuan per month. The workers have now decided to send representatives again to request the union to expedite negotiations to maintain their livelihood.

South District Rent Reduction Committee's Letter to H.E. Gewk-Mi

The Landlord of Nine Acres of Land Has Already Indicated Rent Reduction

The Shanghai South City District Rent Reduction Committee is sparing no effort in its rent reduction appeals. Several hundred new houses in the Nine Acres of Land, Luxiangyuan Road, owned by Anhe Company, are inhabited by middle-class people and above. The Rent Reduction Committee, recognizing the recent rapid appreciation of the Nine Acres of Land's market conditions, sent a letter to Anhe Company requesting a reduction in rent to promote the prosperity of the area. It is reported that after receiving the letter, the company announced yesterday that it would temporarily collect rent at 95% of the original price. In the commercial center area of the British Concession, empty houses stand in rows. The Rent Reduction Committee sent a letter to H.E. Gewk-Mi of Hardoon Realties, requesting that he voluntarily reduce rent. The original letter is recorded below.

Respectfully,

In recent times, the economy of our Chinese people is on the verge of bankruptcy. Both rural and urban areas have been affected. Shanghai, once known as the "Paris of the East," also presents a picture of commercial depression and market stagnation, a far cry from previous years. Even in Shanghai's most prosperous areas, such as the area surrounding Nanjing Road, most of the tall buildings and mansions are owned by Hardoon Realties. Recently, due to poor market conditions and high rents, businesses have closed and people have moved away in large numbers, especially in the new buildings between Great Malu and Second Malu. Before the renovation of that area, its residents and businesses were densely packed. Why was this? Because the rent was low, and there was harmony like in the times of Emperors Yao and Shun. After the renovation, because the rent increased more than tenfold, since its completion several years ago, nine out of ten houses remain empty. Some have tried to pay exorbitant rents in hopes of restoring the area's prosperity, but ultimately, the abundance of empty houses and the scarcity of businesses have led to few pedestrians and reluctant customers. Therefore, high rents are a fatal wound to the market.

The late H.E. Hardoon, a great tycoon in Shanghai, held the leading position in the real estate industry. During his lifetime, he performed numerous good deeds, but it is regrettable that his descendants have not followed in his footsteps. We have long admired your respect for Buddhism and your practice of universal love and benevolence to relieve all suffering. The countless masses are in a hell of hunger, drowning, axes, and drills. We hope that you will uphold the grand aspiration of the compassionate ship and universally liberate them to reach the other shore. Relieving the suffering of the masses is the supreme method. We earnestly request that you consider reducing the rents in various locations of the Hardoon estate, which would conform to the Buddhist teaching of benefiting all beings and the principle of all dharmas returning to oneness. If you could spread the willow branch and make the earth and sky seem vast, and we could appease your heart by pleading for the people, we would bow our heads, put our palms together, and pray, respectfully awaiting your teachings to alleviate our thirst for revival.

Woman Zhang Qiaozhen Sues Wang Wenda for Rape

Postponed for Further Investigation and Trial

Hu Zhucheng, a Ningbo native who works as a teacher at Chonggong Elementary School on Xiaoshadu Road in West Shanghai, married Zhang Qiaozhen, a woman from the same hometown, through a matchmaker three years ago. In July of last year, Wang Wen Da, who worked at Hongshun Foreign Firm on Jiangxi Road, met Zhang Qiaozhen at a playground. They fell in love at first sight and often went out together. Recently, Zhang Qiaozhen reported to the Public Security Bureau that Wang Wen Da had raped her. Wang Wen Da was arrested and handed over to the Local Court because the case involved morality. Prosecutor Du Jiasheng interrogated him and released him on bail. After repeated investigations, he was indicted on charges of disrupting the family. Yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, Judge Chen Kangsun specially opened the Fifth Court for trial.

First, the plaintiff Zhang Qiaozhen testified: I am 20 years old and live at 37 Yuezhou Road. (Question) What are you accusing Wang Wen Da of? (Answer) Wang borrowed 20 yuan from me. I have been pressing him for a long time without success, so I am suing him. (Answer) Why are you accusing him of disrupting the family over a visit to the Da Fang Hotel last July or August? (Answer) Last July or August, Wang wanted to rape me at the Da Fang Hotel. (Question) Did you and Wang stay overnight together? (Answer) No. (Question) Why did you go to the Da Fang Hotel? (Answer) To ask Wang Wen Da for money. (Question) Has this money been returned to you? (Answer) No.

Next, Zhang Yinshi testified: I am 39 years old, a Shanghai native, and live at 3 Wang Yi Ma Lane, No. 3. My husband is a coppersmith. (Question) Who is Zhang Qiaozhen to you? (Answer) My biological daughter. (Question) Has Qiaozhen been married? (Answer) She married a man surnamed Hu three years ago. (Question) What are you accusing Wang Wen Da of? (Answer) I am not accusing him. (Question) Who wrote the complaint? (Answer) I don't know. (Question) What exactly did your daughter quarrel with Wang Wen Da about? (Answer) I don't know.

Finally, Wang Wen Da testified: I am 28 years old, a Ningbo native, and live at 3 Xilin Road, outside Ximen in the South City. (Question) Briefly explain the facts of the crime that happened last July or August. Briefly, Wang Wen Da actually committed the crime under Article 275, Section 2. During the investigation, the plaintiff Zhang Qiaozhen stated that she was a woman under the legal age who was forced into illicit relations by the defendant Wang Wen Da. She never stated that she was already married to Hu Zhu. The defendant also admitted to opening the Da Fang Hotel, and Zhang Qiaozhen also stated that she went to the Da Fang Hotel, etc. The judge believed that the case needed further investigation and postponed the trial. The defendant Wang Wen Da remained on bail.

Autopsy of a Female Hostess

Xu Meiying, a 28-year-old Jiangwan woman who worked as a hostess in the Daxing Class at the Xinxin Company amusement park, residing on the third floor of Yuanshenchang Porcelain Shop, No. 88 Jin Shenfu Road, French Concession, was found dead between 9 and 10 a.m. one day. A man wearing short clothes, about 30 years old, went to her residence and strangled her with a woman's trouser belt before fleeing. At noon, her lover, Gu Xiaodi, returned home and discovered the crime. Gold bracelets, rings, and ornaments worth over 400 yuan, as well as dozens of yuan in cash, were stolen. He immediately reported to the French police, who sent detectives to investigate and transported the body to the morgue for an autopsy. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday, the police reported to the Special Second Court, which appointed Prosecutor Wang Ren, along with a forensic doctor and a clerk, to conduct the autopsy at noon. The autopsy revealed that Xu Meiying had indeed been strangled to death before she died. Gu Xiaodi claimed the body for burial. The police are investigating the case and will bring the perpetrators to justice. It is also reported that according to the second landlord, the murderer resembled a local man surnamed Shen, but his name was unknown. Before the incident, he had repeatedly visited Gu's house and stolen seven yuan from the deceased. He also wanted to invite Gu Xiaodi to work in Nanjing, but the deceased found out and stopped him. Gu and Shen went to Nanjing, and Shen later borrowed money from the deceased but was refused. It is believed that these grievances led to the murder.

Page 12

Lin Su, a Student at the Customs Taxation School, Commits Suicide Due to Mental Derangement

Depressed Due to Repeated Exam Failures

Nervous Breakdown Due to Excessive Studying for the Upcoming Preliminary Exam

Lin Su, a young student from Guangdong, 21 years old, currently a third-year student at the Customs Taxation School at No. 200 Yao Bishop Road in the French Concession, boarded and lodged at the school in Dormitory No. 2 on the second floor. After graduation, he would be selected by the Customs Department to serve as a customs officer in various customs offices. Lin was diligent in his studies, but due to his slow intellect, he repeatedly failed the exams and fell behind. As a result, he was constantly depressed and unhappy. Now, with the preliminary exam approaching, he worked hard but was still worried about failing, leading to overexertion of his brain and mental derangement. Recently, he experienced even more stimulation and suddenly had the thought of ending his life.

One night, at 1:45 a.m. (i.e., on the morning of the 2nd), Lin suddenly got out of bed, went to the kitchen, grabbed a kitchen knife, ran to the rooftop on the second floor, and slashed his neck with the knife, cutting his throat. The wound was about an inch deep. He collapsed in pain. His roommates, Fu Yukui (26 years old, from Beiping) and Yang Junmu (22 years old, from Guangdong), were startled by a loud noise on the rooftop in their sleep. They got up and went outside to check, and saw Lin lying in a pool of blood with blood gushing from the wound. They were greatly alarmed and woke up the other students and rushed to the General Affairs Section to report the incident. They hired a car to send Lin to the General Hospital of the Chinese Red Cross on Haig Road for treatment, but due to the severity of the injury, he died shortly after.

They reported to the French police, who sent detectives to investigate. They also sent the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Sub-Morgue for an autopsy and reported to the Prosecutor's Office of the Special Second District Court to appoint Prosecutor Wang Ren, forensic doctor Wei Ligong, and clerk Peng Yi to inspect the body at noon. The deceased had a bald head, wore a brown velvet Western-style shirt, a wool sweater, a white broadcloth shirt, black serge Western-style trousers, and white canvas sneakers. Blood was still oozing from the wound, and his face and hands were covered in blood. It was a tragic sight.

The officials sat in court, and both Chinese and Western detectives reported the case and the investigation process, and presented the murder weapon. The officials questioned Fu and Yang about the discovery and the deceased's recent circumstances. Lin's fellow student Zhang Runfu from the same hometown stated that the deceased's family was still in his hometown, and he had sent a telegram to inform them. He was willing to be responsible for claiming the body and arranging the burial. The officials ruled that Lin Su had died from a throat injury caused by a knife. The body was allowed to be claimed by Zhang Runfu for burial.

Hungarian-Austrian Painting Exhibition

Opened Yesterday at the American Women's Club

Mayor Wu and Cai Yuanpei Both Attended

Hungarian painter Géza Kádár, along with hundreds of works by famous Hungarian and Austrian artists, came to Shanghai from Europe. With the initiative of the Shanghai Western Art Association and the support of prominent Shanghai figures such as Mayor Wu, Cai Yuanpei, Pan Zhiquan, Ma Yinliang, and Zhang Zhuping, the Hungarian-Austrian painting exhibition was held at the American Women's Club at 577 Jing'an Temple Road. It opened yesterday at 5:30 p.m. and is scheduled to last for two weeks.

Among those who visited yesterday were Mayor Wu and his wife, Cai Yuanpei and his wife, Municipal Government Secretary Tang Shixuan, Li Mu, Polish Minister Weydenthal and his wife, Zhang Zhuping and his wife, famous painters Hu Boxiang, Hu Bozhou, Wu Zhongxiong and his wife, Lang Lusun, and hundreds of foreign merchants from various countries. Hungarian and Austrian works were hung all over the walls, a dazzling array. Most were oil paintings, with unique brushwork and artistic conception, worthy of reference by our country's painters. According to art critics, most of the paintings were above the average level. Kádár personally greeted guests in the hall and gave detailed explanations of each painting, which was very interesting. Madam Wellington Koo, one of the sponsors, also visited to appreciate the works. Around 8 p.m., the guests gradually dispersed. The exhibition is open to the public starting today. Those who wish to purchase paintings can inquire about the prices from Kádár himself.

The Latest Domestically Produced Fire Engine Arrived in Caojiadu Yesterday

Director Xi Yuqing of the Caojiadu Fire Brigade had previously noted that the western Shanghai area was vast, with many factories, and the firefighting equipment was mostly old and dilapidated. He was always uneasy whenever a fire broke out. Last winter, he consulted with the Third District Branch of the Municipal Citizens' Association to discuss purchasing new fire engines. With the permission of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Fire Department and the approval of the Municipal Government, it was decided to add two new fire engines. In addition to the 2,000 yuan raised locally, the remaining funds were allocated from the municipal treasury.

It is now reported that the new fire engine, designed in detail by the Municipal Fire Department, was manufactured by Hengda Machinery Factory, a Chinese-owned enterprise. The Damont type fire engine weighs three tons, is 26 feet long, and over 10 feet high. The ladder is 48 feet high and has three sections. Yesterday morning, it paraded along Bailinan Road, Jessfield Road, and Robison Road. Shops along the way set off firecrackers to welcome it, making it very lively. In the afternoon, it went to the Shanghai West Railway Station and demonstrated a water spray height of 15 feet. Director Yu and all members of the brigade expressed satisfaction. The second new Ketterel type fire engine will be completed by the end of this month. Once it is ready, Mayor Wu will hold a grand completion ceremony. The two fire engines cost a total of 18,000 yuan.

The Weather in This City is Mild and Pleasant

Insects Awaken on the Fifth, the Jingzhe Festival

Pay Attention to Pest Control in the Fields

The weather in this city has been cloudy and hazy in recent days, with very low air pressure, leading to frequent heavy fog, making breathing difficult. Epidemics such as diphtheria and measles have suddenly broken out. However, since the day before yesterday, the weather has cleared up, and the cloudy haze has been swept away. Furthermore, the weather is unusually warm, and citizens have replaced their fur coats with cotton-padded jackets, fully demonstrating the spirit of spring.

It is also learned that the fifth of this month is the Jingzhe Festival, when all insects awaken. Due to the warm and humid weather of the past few days, and the rain and snow in early spring, pests are bound to breed in the fields. Therefore, farmers should start pest control work at this time to avoid harming the harvest.

A Page from the Love Story of a Russian and a German Wife

The Man and Woman Had Been to Qingdao Together

Arrested and Escorted Back to Shanghai for Theft

Russian national Vladimir Mentchougloff (formerly known as the leader of the International Kidnapping Gang), a dentist at 83 Beijing Road (34 years old), met the wife of German national Harsdörffer, living at 612 Enbrook Building, North Suzhou Road, in April of last year when she sought treatment for a toothache. They fell in love. Later, Mentchougloff moved to 1081 North Sichuan Road, and Mrs. Harsdörffer often visited him for chats. On January 10th of this year, the woman and a daughter went to Qingdao with Mentchougloff, carrying many pieces of luggage, without informing her husband (Harsdörffer works at the Syme & Co. Foreign Firm).

Her husband returned home and discovered that a gold ingot worth 7,390 yuan, weighing 70 taels, 43 Japanese gold coins, and two American gold coins, which were hidden in the drawer of a desk in the bedroom, were missing. The drawer showed no signs of forced entry. He reported the incident to the Hongkou Police Station, which obtained an arrest warrant from the First Special District Court and apprehended them in Dalian. They were brought back to Shanghai on the Shanghai Maru and detained at the Hongkou Police Station. They were charged with theft under Article 337, Section 1 of the Criminal Code. The defendant denied stealing the items. The court ordered that Harsdörffer's wife, who had been detained by the Public Security Bureau in Qingdao, be brought to court to testify. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yinghua convened a continued hearing in the Fifth Criminal Court.

Police lawyer Jiang Baolian stated the case, and said that the plaintiff's wife and a Chinese man named Zhang Zifu were present, and could prove everything. Mrs. Harsdörffer, 31 years old, who returned from Qingdao yesterday, testified that she met the defendant in April of last year when she was treated for a dental illness. She saw the gold ingot and Japanese and American gold coins in her husband's drawer in October and found it strange. She mentioned it to the defendant, but her husband kept the drawer key, and the defendant did not know her address, so he had never been to her house. It was not until the third of this month that she learned that she had forgotten a handbag containing a key to the main door at his place in December and had not retrieved it. She had been planning to return to her home country, but her husband did not agree. This time, because of the funeral of Mayers, the director of Syme & Co., she decided to return to her home country for a trip. On the eighth of last month, she discussed it with the defendant, who promised to give her travel expenses and send her to Harbin. Therefore, on the morning of the ninth, when her husband was not at home, she had him hire a car to her door. She had him take away a handbag and a hatbox. The next morning, she left with her daughter and him, first going to Qingdao. She had no knowledge of his theft and did not ask him to do such things.

The local man Zhang Zifu testified that he used to work as a cook at the defendant's place. At the end of last year, he saw him holding a key that looked like the one presented in court and working on it with a file. He asked him what it was for, and he said that he had lost a mailbox key and was making a replacement. He did not know anything else. The owner of the stolen goods, Harsdörffer, testified that although his wife had seen the drawer key, he always kept it in his waistcoat pocket and never gave it to her. Sometimes he put it in a tin box in a small room, but he would usually change clothes and forget to take it out. After a while, he would realize it and put it back in safekeeping.

When questioned, the defendant firmly denied stealing the items and hired a lawyer to request bail to avoid wrongful imprisonment. Judge Xiang granted the request and ordered the defendant to post a cash bail of 7,390 yuan and adjourned the case for further investigation.

Jin Menggen, Who Was Assassinated, Needs an Autopsy to Retrieve the Bullet

The Family Cannot Bear It and Firmly Requests Exemption from Autopsy

Jin Menggen, who opened a teahouse in Zhoujiaqiao, West Shanghai, was friends with Wang Xinshan, who lived nearby. However, they had different opinions and were mutually suspicious. In the winter of the year before last, they jointly opened the Yongle Tanhuang Theater, but there were conflicts over changing the acting troupe. In the first month of the lunar calendar last year, Wang had people disrupt the theater, and Jin drove them away on the spot. Wang Xinshan was very dissatisfied and knew that Jin Menggen carried a birdcage outside every morning. Therefore, he instructed Zhang Pengfei and A Er to lie in wait near Hopeland Road with guns on the morning of June 10th at about 5 a.m.

Soon they saw Jin walking past with a birdcage. Zhang and others opened fire and shot Jin down. Jin's wife, Ms. Bao, heard the news at home and rushed to the scene. Jin was still able to speak and named the murderers in a broken voice. He died shortly after. Afterwards, Jin's wives, Ms. Bao and Ms. Liu, reported the incident to the Sixth District Police Station, which arrested Wang Xinshan and handed him over to the Nanshi Local Court. The court sent personnel to conduct an autopsy. As a result, Wang Xinshan was sentenced to death for premeditated murder. Wang appealed to the Jiangsu High Court, which ordered Wang to be taken to Suzhou for interrogation.

Yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, Judge Shao Qinzhi of the Local Court specially opened the Third Court and ordered Jin Bao and Jin Zhang to appear in court. (Question) How did your husband Jin Menggen die? (Answer) He was shot and killed by Wang Xinshan. (Question) Do you know the current status of the case? (Answer) Because Wang Xinshan did not accept the verdict, he was taken to Suzhou and is currently being tried by the High Court. (Question) Because the bullet fired into your husband's abdomen has not been removed, this court intends to send your husband's coffin to the Zhenru Forensic Institute to extract the bullet for research. Upon hearing this, Jin Bao and others replied, "My husband suffered a tragic gunshot death and died miserably. Please ask the presiding judge to exempt us from the autopsy." The judge said, "Could it be that you have already reached an agreement outside?" The two women replied together, "There has been no contact. We request an exemption from the autopsy because we really cannot bear to move the body again. We have no other intention." The judge, upon hearing their testimony, ordered them to leave and await instructions.

Wife Commits Suicide Due to Husband's Unemployment

The Hardships of Life Are Too Horrific to Describe

Zhang Zishi, a 37-year-old woman from Xinghua, lived at No. 604 Taihe Lane, Xiaoshadu Road. Her husband, Zhang Dixin, used to work in a silk factory, but had been unemployed for over a year. The family's livelihood depended on Ms. Zhang's work at the Meifeng Silk Weaving Factory, but her income was meager, leading to extreme financial difficulties and frequent threats of running out of food. Ms. Zhang, seeing that her husband had no suitable employment, thought about the long days ahead and how to survive. Out of resentment, she suddenly had the thought of ending her life and secretly swallowed opium to kill herself. Her husband discovered it and reported to the Gordon Road Police Station, which sent Detective Tao Afu to investigate. They sent her to Guangren Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective. She died at about 3 a.m. yesterday.

The body was transported to the Pailon Road Morgue. At about 10 a.m., Prosecutor Song Gengshan, appointed by the First Special District Local Court, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. After hearing Zhang Dixin's statement of the events, Prosecutor Song ruled that the deceased Zhang Zishi, a female, had indeed died from opium poisoning. The body was handed over to her husband, Zhang Dixin, for burial.

Dredging Copper Sand and Shuan Sand Waterways

Customs House Installs Buoy Lights to Indicate Navigation Routes

The Copper Sand Waterway and the Shuan Sand Waterway of the Yangtze River's southern channel are currently being dredged. As the Jianghai Customs considers this area a crucial navigation channel, it has added buoy lights to indicate the routes. The decided additions are: (1) An upstream buoy light, decorated in red, flashing a white light every eight seconds (four seconds on, four seconds off). This is to guide upstream vessels to navigate the right side of the waterway. It is located at 240 degrees north of the Nanhuizhuang, a distance of 7.15 nautical miles. (2) A middle buoy light, in black with a yellow top, also flashing once every eight seconds, indicating the northern edge of the dredged waterway area. (3) A downstream buoy light, also red, flashing every eight seconds, guiding downstream vessels to navigate the right side of the waterway. It is located at 247 degrees, a distance of 8.58 nautical miles. Furthermore, the ninth section of the sandbar buoy light has been moved to 244 degrees to guide upstream vessels navigating the right side of the waterway. The Copper Sand Shoal buoy light has also been moved to 257 degrees, a distance of 12.10 nautical miles. All ships are hereby notified that these changes will take effect on the 28th of this month.

French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association Protests Detectives' Abuse of Power

Yesterday Sent Letter to Police Commissioner Requesting Thorough Investigation and Reply

Search Warrants Should Be Obtained from the Court for Searches

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association, acting on behalf of the Fourth District Branch of the Second Special District Citizens United Association, reported that Mr. Dong Wenli, a Standing Committee member, was falsely accused by a French police Inspector Qian, who incited an apprentice to harm a legitimate merchant. Yesterday, they sent a letter to the French Police Commissioner protesting and requesting a thorough investigation and reply. The original text is recorded below: To the esteemed Commissioner: We received a letter dated February 17th from the Fourth District Branch of the Second Special District Citizens United Association stating that Mr. Wang Lianqing of Wang Shunqing Wood Shop at 206 Pingji Road reported that on the night of the 13th of this month at 8 p.m., a large number of French police detectives suddenly searched the shop, claiming to be catching gamblers. At the time, four tenants were playing mahjong upstairs. The detectives searched upstairs but found nothing. They told the four people that playing mahjong was not an arrestable offense, but shortly after leaving, they returned and arrested all four of them. They also dragged Wang Wenqing, an apprentice who was already in bed, out of bed. Chinese Inspector Qian Chenglong threatened him with a gun, ordering the apprentice to reveal the gambling den. The apprentice said he didn't know, so he was beaten and kicked arbitrarily. Subsequently, the group was detained in the police station. The apprentice was locked in a room and incited to confess that Dong Wenli ran a gambling den, and then released, the apprentice, being ignorant, could only say yes or no. The next day, the five men were released. At the same time, Mr. Dong Wenli, a Standing Committee member of this association, also reported that the police had sent detectives to search and monitor his activities and requested us to negotiate reasonably. Based on this, our association conducted a detailed investigation and convened an emergency meeting. It was agreed that the French police often base searches of residences on anonymous letters. If they find nothing, they arbitrarily insult people. If they find something, they exaggerate the matter and ensure that the person is convicted. It is requested that a letter be forwarded to the Second Special District Court so that in the future, the French police must obtain a search warrant from the court before conducting a search to prevent citizens from being disturbed without reason and from being framed. As for Inspector Qian Chenglong leading detectives to search shops, treating mahjong as gambling, arbitrarily arresting ignorant apprentices, and falsely accusing legitimate merchants, and subsequently fabricating various charges in order to trap Mr. Dong, such abuse of power is lawless. It is requested that a letter be forwarded to the French Chief Secretary General requesting a thorough investigation to ensure the safety of merchants. If there is no response, it is requested that a letter be forwarded to the French Consul General to order an investigation. In addition to sending letters to various groups requesting assistance, a letter is being sent to your association to request negotiation. The letter arrived at the association more than ten days ago. The association believes that the case is significant and has conducted repeated detailed investigations. According to reports from various parties, the case involves fabricated facts and false accusations against merchants. If it is not investigated truthfully, the citizens of the concession will inevitably be in a state of constant fear. Based on the above investigation, we urgently write to your esteemed Commissioner, requesting a thorough investigation and requesting a detailed report of the investigation to be forwarded so that we can inform the relevant parties. To the Police Commissioner of the French Concession.

Planned Renovation of Yantang Road in Zhuanqiao

Construction to Begin Immediately After Survey Completion

The Zhuanqiao Town Plan in Shanghai County was previously established by the county government and submitted to the Provincial Department of Construction for approval. The original Yantang Road is rugged and muddy, making travel inconvenient. The 22nd Rural Improvement Conference of the Zhuanqiao Farmers' Education Center proposed renovation. It has now been decided to widen and raise a section from the entrance of Xindong Street to the Wangjiazhai boundary with the Second District, and the plan has been reported to the county government for approval. The county government recently sent technical directors Qi Kezhong and Ling Jin, equipped with surveying instruments, to Zhuanqiao to measure the road surface. The work was completed at dusk. This section of the project is 1.8 kilometers long and will require the construction of one bridge and eight culverts, with three obstacles. Change of Director at Zhabei Civilian Education Center

New Director's Inauguration Ceremony Held Yesterday

The Zhabei Liuying Road Civilian Education Center, under the Shanghai Local Association, was transferred to the Chinese Children's Welfare Association last autumn due to financial difficulties. The association's Executive Committee, considering that the majority of the center's students are children under the age of 20, which falls within the association's scope of relief, appointed Wang Guanyi, a staff member of the Protection Group, to serve concurrently as the director of the education center. Director Wang Guanyi assumed office on August 1st of last year, and more than half a year has passed in a flash. Recently, the Management Committee members held a meeting and unanimously agreed that Wang Guanyi's concurrent position as director of the education center was inappropriate as it meant abandoning his original child protection duties. Therefore, it was decided to replace Wang Guanyi and appoint Wang Zhenchang as the director of the education center. This decision was formally approved by the Executive Committee. Suicide at Yong'an Hotel

A Suicide Note Claimed Overwhelming Debt

A traveler came to the Yong'an Hotel on Maigen Road at around 4 p.m. the day before yesterday and said he wanted to stay. The hotel accountant led him to Room 30. The guest claimed to be named Ying San囡, from Changzhou, 36 years old, and engaged in the tricycle business. He closed the door and went to sleep that night without any other abnormalities. Unexpectedly, at around 11 a.m. yesterday morning, the hotel tea server knocked on the door to ask if the room was still needed when he suddenly heard a moaning sound from inside. He became suspicious and pushed the door open. He saw Ying San囡 lying across the bed, his face pale and blood frothing from his mouth. He pushed him but could not wake him up. Knowing that something had happened, he quickly reported to the local police station, which sent a car to rush him to Renji Hospital for treatment. It was learned that he had taken poison. However, due to the excessive amount, his life was in danger. Afterwards, the police found a suicide note next to him, addressed to Ying's mother-in-law, who lives in the Qinkong Umbrella Factory in Yongji Lane on Xin Zha Road in this city. The letter stated that he was in overwhelming debt and unable to repay it, so he had no choice but to commit suicide.

Police Chief Courageously Captures Three Thieves in Theft on MacLeod Road

The Zhonghua Drilling Company on MacLeod Road in Huxi was founded by an American. The area is remote and sparsely populated, surrounded by wilderness, making it a target for thieves. Thefts have occurred repeatedly last winter. At 3:30 a.m. the day before yesterday, seven or eight thieves suddenly arrived, each holding iron bars and bamboo poles, and smashed the company's gate. They then rushed in, intending to start looting. Fortunately, Police Chief Liu Shaoquan of the local guard station happened to be patrolling with his police officers. When the thieves saw the police arrive, they knew they had failed and immediately retreated and fled. The police bravely went forward to pursue them. Unexpectedly, the thieves dared to resist arrest, and a rain of clubs and poles fell. Police Chief Liu was seriously injured in the left arm. The police arrested three thieves and took them to the Pusong Police Station. Dong, the station chief, interrogated the thieves. One, Li Hujin, one, Feng Jisheng, and one, Shen Litang, all confessed to conspiring to commit robbery and resisting arrest, and injuring the police chief. Yesterday, a document was prepared and they were sent to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Husband Has Hidden Illness, Wife Seeks Divorce

Xu Yonghuang, a 21-year-old Suzhou native residing at 339, Lane 689, Zhaofeng Road, Hongkou, married Fu Juying, a woman from Yuyao, through a matchmaker. The wedding ceremony was held on December 2nd of last year at the Xin Xin Restaurant, with Le Zhenbao, a well-known businessman, as the witness. Unexpectedly, after living together, Fu discovered that her husband suffered from a hidden illness, and she became unhappy and resentful. As a result, the relationship between the two deteriorated. The woman returned to her parents' home before a month had passed. Recently, she hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the First Special District Local Court, requesting a divorce. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Qiao Wanxuan held a hearing. The plaintiff did not appear. According to her lawyer, the marriage between the plaintiff and the defendant was solely arranged by the plaintiff's uncle, Fu Yuxiang, because he had a close relationship with the defendant's father. He sacrificed his niece for this relationship. The lawyer said that after the plaintiff married, she immediately discovered that the defendant had a hidden illness, which caused her deep resentment. The defendant repeatedly abused her with his parents, making it difficult for the plaintiff to live with him. After she returned to her mother's home, the defendant came to threaten her. Therefore, she had no choice but to file for divorce. However, the defendant Xu Yonghuang denied all three accusations made by the plaintiff: that he suffered from a hidden illness, repeatedly abused her, and frequently threatened her. He also filed a counterclaim, requesting that the court order them to live together. Judge Qiao believed that since the plaintiff had not appeared in court in person, it was not easy to understand the facts, so he postponed the hearing and ordered the plaintiff to appear in court for further questioning.

Rickshaw Puller Becomes Robber

Snatches French Soldier's Wallet

Sentenced to Six Months Imprisonment as a Warning

French sailor Stephane Oulf rode in a rickshaw pulled by Cao Sanwen, a Jiangbei native, from the Bund on Guangdong Road to near Fair Road and Broadway Road at around 8 p.m. the day before yesterday. He gave him two cents for the fare. Cao complained that it was too little. The French soldier took out his wallet from his pocket and added two cents. Cao saw that there were 26 yuan in the wallet. He was overcome with greed and snatched the wallet and fled. The French soldier chased after him and grabbed him. Cao threw back six yuan. The other 20 yuan were taken by his accomplices. Chinese detective Liu Binshan saw this and took him to the Huishan Police Station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Criminal Court 3 of the First Special Court. Labor Bureau lawyer Li Zhichen stated the facts. The French soldier did not appear due to other matters. Judge Wu Zehan interrogated the defendant and sentenced Cao Sanwen to six months' imprisonment as a warning.

Gambling Den Raided in Nine Acres

Twenty-Three Male Gamblers

Gambling Equipment and Smoking Paraphernalia All Present

Lu, the captain of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's detective team, learned that Chen Yongfu, a well-known gangster (nicknamed "Shorty Yongfu," who usually cheated people out of their money with loaded dice, active dominoes, and other fake gambling equipment) was gathering people to gamble and taking a cut in a building at 7 Yi'an Lane in Nine Acres, gambling all night long. He offered gambling on various games such as dice, Pai Gow, and Mahjong. He immediately dispatched detectives Wu Songshan and others to cooperate with the police chief of the Chenxiangge Police Station and rushed to the scene at 4:30 p.m. yesterday. At that time, the gamblers were enthusiastically calling out and drinking, and they had also privately set up smoking couches to sell opium. On the spot, they arrested 23 male and female gamblers, including You Chen and others, and took them, along with dice, dominoes, Mahjong tiles, and smoking paraphernalia such as opium pipes and lamps, to the Chenxiangge Police Station. Chief Shen ordered them to be detained for preliminary examination before being sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

A fire broke out suddenly at the Lisheng Celluloid Factory at 832 Manufacturing Bureau Road in Nanshi at 6:10 p.m. yesterday. Flames and smoke soared into the sky. The fire brigade drove to the scene and extinguished the fire after exerting all their efforts. As a result, six factory buildings were burned down.

A fire suddenly broke out in a certain family's residence at 64, Lane 57, Qiqihar Road at 8:50 p.m. yesterday. Thick smoke spread everywhere, and the fire was very fierce, quickly spreading to numbers 66 and 68 next door. The fire brigade was alerted and drove to the scene to put out the fire. A fire broke out accidentally in a bungalow at numbers 57 and 66 on Ward Road in Pudong at around 9:15 p.m. last night. Flames suddenly burst through the roof and spread in all directions, burning numbers 64 and 66 on either side. The fire brigade rushed to the scene and put out the fire. It took an hour to extinguish. Three houses were burned.

Inspector General of the Special Agency of the French Concession Police, Jin Jiulin, Detective Zhang Ziying, Deputy Detective Qin Youyu, Plainclothes Detectives Ma Yizhi, Xu Youyi, Zhu Juotong, and others apprehended a bandit named Yu Youfa (from Anhui) at Caishi Road at 7 PM the day before yesterday. They confiscated a pistol and four bullets. He was taken to the police station and confessed that from June of last year to January of this year, he had colluded with accomplices to rob eleven residences and shops, including No. 259 Fulililu Road, No. 272 of the same road, No. 134 Xujiahui Road, No. 127 of the same road, No. 329 of the same road, No. 34 of the same road, No. 469 Caishi Road, No. 407 of the same road, No. 437 Jin Shenfu Road, a certain address on Gaoen Road, and others. He admitted to dividing the stolen goods and spending the money. The police chief ordered him to be detained. Yesterday, he was sent to the First Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. The police lawyer, Yao Zhaodi, explained the case and requested a postponement to arrest the accomplices who are still at large and conduct a detailed investigation before filing a lawsuit. He also presented the pistol and bullets as evidence. Judge Li Changnian reviewed the report, briefly questioned the defendant, and then approved a postponement of fifteen days for further questioning. The defendant was returned to custody.

Establishment of Branch Unions at the Zhabei Railway Union Today

Since the Special Party Department of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Unions dispatched members to reorganize the union according to law, the reorganization office of the union has been actively proceeding. Eleven branch unions of the two railways have been established. On the Beijing-Shanghai line, the Wusong, Nanjing, and Meggen Road branches have already been established. The Shanghai-Hangzhou line originally had four branch unions, with the Zhabei branch having the largest number of members. It is now learned that this branch is also ready and will elect branch union officers by direct election. The inaugural meeting will be held today (March 3rd) at 1 PM in Zhabei. The Shubaoku Hezuoshe bookstore, located at No. 243 Wangping Street in Shanghai, has seen its publication of the "Twenty-Six Histories" become popular at home and abroad. Now, it is also selling a special-priced edition of the Song Dynasty edition of the "Four Histories" in four exquisitely bound volumes for only ten yuan per set, which can be described as both inexpensive and high-quality. At the same time, it is also compiling and printing the "Historical Studies Series," which currently includes "Chronicles of Arts and Literature of Chinese Dynasties," "Chronicles of Food and Commodities of Chinese Dynasties" (also known as "Materials for Chinese Economic History"), "Chronicles of Foreign Peoples of Chinese Dynasties," and "Chronicles of Official Positions of Chinese Dynasties." These four types extract important historical materials from the "Twenty-Six Histories" and "Nine Compendia" into one book, which is truly great news for the cultural world.

Zhongshan Association Holds Membership Drive

The Shanghai Zhongshan Native Place Association was virtually suspended during the Songhu Battle. Last winter, a general meeting of Zhongshan natives in Shanghai was convened, and a reorganization committee was formed to rigorously reorganize the association. Since then, this long-dormant Zhongshan Native Place Association has seen a glimmer of hope. Recently, work has been stepped up, with both a general registration of members and a membership drive being conducted. As a result, the atmosphere has been revitalized and spirits greatly boosted. Several hundred natives of Zhongshan with both reputation and popularity in Shanghai have been hired to serve as captains of the solicitation teams, and a general headquarters for membership solicitation has been established within the association's premises on Qiujiang Road in Zhabei. The solicitation work has begun and is extremely intense. According to the plan, there are two types of memberships: Type A members pay an admission fee of five yuan, and Type B members pay one yuan. During the solicitation period, both are reduced by half.

Sun Honglin, a judge of the Criminal Division of the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, received an order from the Ministry of Judicial Administration stating that due to the large number of appeals from various provinces to the Supreme Court recently, the original judges of each division were unable to handle them. The vacancy will be temporarily filled by Xiong Huiping, a judge of the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court, as ordered by Liang, the president of the Third Branch of the High Court. The vacancy left by Xiong will be filled by someone assigned by President Wang Simo. Sun and Xiong, upon receiving the order, immediately exchanged and handled the documents and will go to their new positions to work tomorrow or the day after.

Skota Cup Semi-Final Replay: Tung Wah Eliminated Lux

3-2

Winning the Right to Play French Club in the Final

Both Sides Perform Extremely Well

Over Ten Thousand People at the Recreation Ground Cheer Enthusiastically

The Skota Cup semi-final replay between Tung Wah and Lux, after a 2-2 draw the previous week, was fiercely contested again yesterday at the Recreation Ground. Tung Wah finally eliminated Lux with a score of 3-2, winning the right to play the French Club in the final. Yesterday, the spring sunshine was bright, and the weather was mild. No less than ten thousand people, both men and women, were in the stands at the Recreation Ground, all cheering enthusiastically and gleefully.

Tung Wah Players Give Their All

Tung Wah had been conserving their energy for a long time and were in high spirits with a neat military appearance. Although Guan Xun'an had not returned from the Fudan expedition to the north, and Chen Hongguang was unable to rush back in time, their strength was not affected. Moreover, Feng Yunyou gave an especially strong performance, looking ahead and behind, responding to all sides, and running tirelessly. Except for Wan Xianghua, who was slightly lacking, the five forwards all worked hard, giving their all. Jia Youliang's right wing had reached the point of perfection, sending out many brilliant balls and giving Dai Li many opportunities. However, Lu Zhongen's carelessness caused an accident, leading to the tense situation of 3-2.

Lux Put on a Deep Performance

Lux were all young and brave generals, with talent just like Tung Wah. Recently, they had been winning every game. Even the Western police acknowledged their defeat. They were generally recognized as the only strong team among Westerners. After drawing 2-2 with Tung Wah the previous week, they were ambitious and hoped to win the Skota Cup. Therefore, when old enemies met again, a fierce battle was inevitable. Sure enough, they were the first to break through Tung Wah's defense, but in the end, they were defeated by a difference of one goal. The performances of Rumons, H. Mada, Bosalie, and goalkeeper Kokren were commendable and gave the audience a deep impression.

Bosalie Actually Scores First

After the two teams were photographed, Tung Wah kicked off from the east to attack. The spectators cheered wildly, and the atmosphere in the stadium was very tense. Feng Yunyou kicked a free kick, forcing it to the baseline. Wan Xianghua sent out a corner kick, and Chen Jia's header was cleverly caught by Kokren. Tung Wah continued to attack fiercely, and the situation in front of Lux's goal was precarious. Li Yichen and Dai Linjing made several attempts to score, but they were unsuccessful. After Lux overcame the difficulties, they suddenly became like unbridled horses, moving straight ahead and launching an offensive. The forwards were extremely fast, and Tung Wah's hinterland was in great urgency. Bosalie appeared and disappeared unpredictably, entering every gap. Lu Zhongen failed to save the ball, and Little Bao caught up and kicked it into the net. Tung Wah was actually the first to lose a goal.

Li Yichen Returns the Favor

Since Tung Wah had lost the first goal, the spectators were all shocked. Even the Tung Wah players were like frightened birds. Fortunately, their military appearance was neat and orderly, and they were careful. Jia Youliang sent a high ball from the boundary, and Dai Linjing responded in the center, attacking the goal unsuccessfully. Feng Yunyou made a comeback, and the high ball was picked up and passed over Jia Youliang's head. Li Yichen got what he wanted and shot at the goal, establishing a great feat and creating a tie. The audience was filled with joy again, and the atmosphere turned milder. But from then on, the competitive situation became even more intense.

Two to One, Tung Wah Takes the Lead

The connection between the two teams was good, and their actions were fast. It was truly a rare and wonderful game. Lux tried hard to attack, and the three forwards were extremely hardworking, but the two wings were slightly weak. Based on the mistakes of the past, Tung Wah built high walls and deep trenches, paying special attention to defense. Therefore, Lux's several attempts to probe were unsuccessful. Wan Xianghua stole in along the side and shot, but it was caught. Feng Yunyou got the ball and passed it to Jia Youliang, who crossed from the baseline. Li Yichen forwarded it to Dai Linjing. A'Dai aimed at the enemy's goal and built another achievement. Thus, they turned defeat into victory, and the first half ended with a score of 2-1.

Li Yichen Creates Three to One

After the break, Lux tried to win with surprise tactics, but after T. Mada's corner kick failed, Tung Wah was given the opportunity to attack. Dai Linjing led the army forward. Jia Youliang dribbled the ball deep into the side of the goal, but he was too close and could not use it. After more than ten minutes, Lux's actions were slightly out of order. Tung Wah did not take it to heart and fought calmly. Jia Youliang passed a ball, Dai Linjing feinted, and Li Yichen shot it in, making it 3-1. Tung Wah then occupied an extremely advantageous position.

Lux's Last Struggle

Lux's arrogance declined slightly, and Tung Wah's limelight was strong. It seemed that they could rest easy. Li Yichen got the ball from Youliang and flew it into the sky, missing the opportunity. Lux attacked several times, but there was no way in. After a long battle, Simmons struggled hard to create an opportunity. Bosalie was eager to try, but he failed to score several times. Later, due to A'Lu's carelessness, Bao was finally able to build another achievement, ending the game with a score of 3-2. The players from both teams were as follows:

Tung Wah Club

Lu Zhongen, Li Ning, Chen Gongyu, Gu Shangxiang, Feng Yunyou, Ding Zhaocheng, Wan Xianghua, Li Yichen, Dai Linjing, Chen Jiaqiu, Jia Youliang

Lux

W. Kokren, Logan, Stand, Guglif, Simmons, H. Mada, Lian, Bosalie, H. Kokren, Atig, T. Mada

International Basketball First Game: China Loses to the United States

The Strength of the United States is Unprecedented

China Remains the Same, Unable to Do Anything

The Result is 57 to 31

This year's Shanghai International Basketball Tournament was disappointing because the women's tournament was suspended due to inconsistent rules. In the men's group, only China and the United States adopted a best-of-three series to determine the winner. China was far from being a match for the United States, which can be said to be extremely disappointing. The sluggishness of the basketball world is lamentable. But comparatively speaking, Chinese basketball skills are not weaker than in previous years. It is only because the American team's basketball skills have improved a lot, resulting in a huge gap. In the first game between China and the United States last night, China lost 31-57. In the first half, the United States scored 31 points, while China only scored 8 points.

The Strongest Lineup in Shanghai

The American team used West Qing Shi Misi, Ranyi, and Karl Sen as three, and Si Jia, with Mai Ling, Lek, and Boli Shi as two capable generals. Such a strong lineup is unprecedented in Shanghai. The accuracy of shooting, the beauty of the connection, and the strictness of the defense are truly admirable. It is no wonder that the Chinese team was at a loss and acknowledged defeat.

China Can Do Nothing

Comparatively speaking, the Chinese lineup was more organized with Feng Nianhua and Qian Jingyong as the two forwards, Lu Zhongen and Sun Baoqing as the guards, and Xu Heng as the center. Chen Zongqi's inner guard can replace Sun Baoqing, but the various aspects of the connection are slightly lacking. Qian Jingyong's basketball skills are far from what they used to be. Feng Nianhua and Sun Baoqing are as they were in the past. Lu Zhongen's prestige is still not reduced, and it is still up to him to command everything.

Only One Shot Made

After the start, the United States came out with a formal lineup, leaving China with no way out and unable to do anything. After four to zero, Sun Baoqing scored the only goal in the first half. After that, it became ten to two. China scored three points by free throws, making it ten to five. Until twenty-six to five, the United States repeatedly changed players. In addition to Sun scoring one goal, China scored six points from free throws. The first half ended with China trailing 8-31.

The Final Situation is Average

Starting in the second half, the American lineup was greatly adjusted. Only Smith of the official personnel remained. After Lu Zhongen scored two consecutive goals, the momentum rose. After that, both sides made progress, and the situation became balanced. Thirty-seven to seventeen, forty-one to twenty-three. This was the closest period of the score. The United States again greatly adjusted its personnel, and the initial five players came on the field again, but the situation was far less tense than before. China also occasionally scored, but in the end, China still lost by as much as twenty-six points, with a score of 31-57. The referees were Zhang Guoxun and Hall. The second game is scheduled for 8 PM on the afternoon of the 6th at the Shen Garden.
